namespace = c3rd_other_events
#Some event to add changes
c3rd_other_events.1 = {
	#Empire leader has too low martial in a war
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.1.t"
	desc = {
		desc = "c3rd_other_events.1.desc"
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				any_country_culture = {
					is_integrated = yes
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:hellenic
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.1.desc.1"
		}
	}
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		is_monarchy = yes
		OR = {
			government = imperium
			country_culture_group = hellenic
		}
		rank = great_power
		current_ruler = {
			martial < 9
		}
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_1
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_2
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_3
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 1050.1.1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_3
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 900.1.1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_2
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_1
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_culture_group = hellenic
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
		}
		add_stability = -5
	}
	option = {
		#please help me improve
		name = c3rd_other_events.1.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.1.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			any_character = {
				has_any_military_office_trigger = yes
				martial > root.current_ruler.martial
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = -25
		current_ruler = {
			add_martial = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ok, don't care
		name = c3rd_other_events.1.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.1.b.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
			add_prominence = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_culture = {
				limit = {
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:hellenic
				}
				add_country_culture_modifier = {
					name = "unworthy_ruler_tradition"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#i'm pretty smooth
		name = c3rd_other_events.1.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.1.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				popularity >= 50
				charisma >= 10
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = 10
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.2 = {
	#removing it
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.2.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.2.desc"
	picture = greek_court
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_1
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_2
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_3
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		current_ruler = {
			save_scope_as = currentruler
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_1
			}
			remove_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_2
			}
			remove_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_3
			}
			remove_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_culture = {
				limit = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = unworthy_ruler_tradition
				}
				remove_country_culture_modifier = unworthy_ruler_tradition
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.2.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.2.a.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.3 = {
	#Divine imperium leader has too low zeal in a war
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.3.t"
	desc = {
		desc = "c3rd_other_events.3.desc"
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				any_country_culture = {
					is_integrated = yes
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:north_african
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.3.desc.1"
		}
	}
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		is_monarchy = yes
		OR = {
			government = imperial_cult
			country_culture_group = north_african
			has_law = elevate_monarch_monarchy
		}
		rank = great_power
		current_ruler = {
			zeal < 9
		}
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_1
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_2
			has_country_modifier = unworthy_leader_3
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 1050.1.1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_3
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 900.1.1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_2
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unworthy_leader_1
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_culture_group = north_african
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
		}
		add_stability = -5
	}
	option = {
		#please help me improve
		name = c3rd_other_events.3.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.3.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			any_character = {
				has_any_religious_office_trigger = yes
				zeal > root.current_ruler.zeal
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = -25
		current_ruler = {
			add_zeal = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ok, don't care
		name = c3rd_other_events.3.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.3.b.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
			add_prominence = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_culture = {
				limit = {
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:north_african
				}
				add_country_culture_modifier = {
					name = "unworthy_ruler_tradition"
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#i'm pretty smooth
		name = c3rd_other_events.3.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.3.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				popularity >= 50
				charisma >= 10
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = 10
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.4 = {
	#social crisis : too few integrated (nobles) pops
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.4.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.4.desc"
	picture = persia_marching
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		rank = great_power
		OR = {
			AND = {
				country_culture_group = latin
				country_population > noble_country_check_italian
			}
			country_population > noble_country_check
		}
		is_ai = no
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = administrative_difficulty
			has_country_modifier = administrative_difficulty_small
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			country_population > noble_country_check_a_lot
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stability <= 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			stability >= 60
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		ordered_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_pop_type_right = nobles
				}
			}
			max = 1
			order_by = country_culture_pop_count
			save_scope_as = chosen_new_nobles
		}
	}
	option = {
		#new elite
		name = c3rd_other_events.4.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.4.a.tt1
		culture_state_loyalty_effect_c3rd = yes
		scope:chosen_new_nobles = {
			if = {
				#workaround if things bug
				limit = {
					root = {
						primary_culture = scope:chosen_new_nobles.culture
					}
				}
				root = {
					random_country_culture = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								this = scope:chosen_new_nobles
							}
						}
						save_scope_as = culture_debug
					}
					set_primary_culture = scope:culture_debug.culture
					set_primary_culture = scope:chosen_new_nobles.culture
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_country_culture_right = nobles
				add_country_culture_modifier = {
					name = "new_culture_elite"
					duration = 1825
				}
				add_country_culture_modifier = {
					name = "promoted_administrators_in_subcultures"
					duration = -1
				}
				custom_tooltip = culture_group_boosted_c3rd_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					root = {
						every_country_culture = {
							limit = {
								this.culture.culture_group = scope:chosen_new_nobles.culture.culture_group
								NOT = {
									this = scope:chosen_new_nobles
								}
								NOT = {
									has_country_culture_modifier = administrators_cultmodifier
								}
							}
							add_country_culture_modifier = {
								name = "administrators_cultmodifier"
								duration = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#refuse
		name = c3rd_other_events.4.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.4.b.tt1
		scope:chosen_new_nobles = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = "new_elite_refused"
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = administrative_difficulty
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	option = {
		#half
		name = c3rd_other_events.4.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.4.c.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				OR = {
					finesse >= 10
					has_trait = crafty
					has_trait = intelligent
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = administrative_difficulty_small
			}
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -5
		}
		add_political_influence = -25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = administrative_difficulty_small
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.5 = {
	#inform about deflation
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.5.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.5.desc"
	picture = aqueducts
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = deflation_value
		var:deflation_value >= 5
		NOT = {
			has_variable = deflation_is_happening
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = deflation_is_happening
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.5.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.5.a.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.6 = {
	#gold mine exhaustion
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.6.t"
	desc = {
		desc = "c3rd_other_events.6.desc"
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				scope:exhausted_mine = {
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = deep_mining
					}
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.6.desc.1"
		}
	}
	picture = war_chest
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		any_owned_province = {
			trade_goods = precious_metals
			has_variable = mine_exhaustion
			var:mine_exhaustion >= 50
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				trade_goods = precious_metals
				has_variable = mine_exhaustion
				var:mine_exhaustion >= 50
			}
			save_scope_as = exhausted_mine
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.6.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.6.a.tt1
		scope:exhausted_mine = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = mine_exhaustion
				}
				remove_variable = mine_exhaustion
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = deep_mining
				}
				remove_province_modifier = deep_mining
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 20
						terrain = plains
					}
					set_trade_goods = horses
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 20
						terrain = forest
					}
					set_trade_goods = wood
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 30
						terrain = farmland
						has_province_rank = settlement
					}
					set_trade_goods = grain
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 30
						terrain = marsh
						has_province_rank = settlement
					}
					set_trade_goods = fish
				}
				20 = {
					modifier = {
						add = 20
						has_province_rank = settlement
					}
					set_trade_goods = base_metals
				}
				5 = {
					set_trade_goods = marble
				}
				5 = {
					set_trade_goods = iron
				}
				5 = {
					set_trade_goods = amber
				}
				10 = {
					set_trade_goods = stone
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.6.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.6.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:exhausted_mine = {
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = deep_mining
				}
			}
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -10
		}
		add_political_influence = -20
		scope:exhausted_mine = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = deep_mining
				duration = -1
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = mine_exhaustion
				add = -20
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.7 = {
	#inform about deflation stopping
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.7.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.7.desc"
	picture = road_construction
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = deflation_value
		var:deflation_value <= 0
		has_variable = deflation_is_happening
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_variable = deflation_is_happening
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.7.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.7.a.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.8 = {
	#event where people are not happy about taxes
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.8.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.8.desc"
	picture = senator_conversing
	left_portrait = scope:character_taxed_1
	right_portrait = scope:character_taxed_2
	right_portrait = scope:character_taxed_3
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		has_country_modifier = tax_inspection
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = citizen_exemption_from_census_tax
			has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			has_variable = remove_tax_inspection_asked
		}
		any_character = {
			count >= 3
			power_base >= 1
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_general = yes
					is_governor = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_country_modifier = political_unstability
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_country_modifier = provinces_republican_reforms
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_modifier = military_advantages
			has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			legitimacy >= 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			legitimacy >= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			legitimacy <= 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			legitimacy <= 0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability <= 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability <= 20
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = remove_tax_inspection_asked
			days = 3650
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_1
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				NOT = {
					this = scope:character_taxed_1
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_2
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				NOR = {
					this = scope:character_taxed_1
					this = scope:character_taxed_2
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					#*2
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_3
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ok
		name = c3rd_other_events.8.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.8.a.tt1
		remove_country_modifier = tax_inspection
		set_variable = {
			name = tax_inspection_stopped
			days = 3650
		}
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
	}
	option = {
		#take my money and shutup
		name = c3rd_other_events.8.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.8.b.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 15
			add_popularity = -10
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = root.has_monthly_income
			multiply = 15
		}
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 5
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 5
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 5
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = deflation_value
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = deflation_value
					add = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no way
		name = c3rd_other_events.8.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.8.c.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 15
		}
		add_stability = -5
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied

c3rd_other_events.9 = {
	#event where people ask for census taxes
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.9.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.9.desc"
	picture = senator_conversing
	left_portrait = scope:character_taxed_1
	right_portrait = scope:character_taxed_2
	right_portrait = scope:character_taxed_3
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = citizen_exemption_from_census_tax
			has_country_modifier = tax_inspection
			has_variable = remove_tax_inspection_asked
			has_variable = census_exemption_asked
			has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		}
		any_character = {
			count >= 3
			power_base >= 1
			is_ruler = no
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					root = {
						has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_general = yes
					is_governor = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_country_modifier = provinces_republican_reforms
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_country_modifier = political_unstability
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_modifier = military_advantages
			has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_monarchy = yes
			legitimacy >= 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_monarchy = yes
			legitimacy >= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_monarchy = yes
			legitimacy <= 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_republic = yes
			has_senate_approval <= 0.4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			is_monarchy = yes
			legitimacy <= 0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			is_republic = yes
			has_senate_approval <= 0.2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability <= 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability <= 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			current_date >= 1000.1.1
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = census_exemption_asked
			days = 3650
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				is_ruler = no
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_1
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					this = scope:character_taxed_1
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_2
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				power_base >= 1
				is_ruler = no
				NOR = {
					this = scope:character_taxed_1
					this = scope:character_taxed_2
				}
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
				modifier = {
					add = corruption
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = righteous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.7
					has_trait = guileless
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_trait = honest
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = character_taxed_3
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ok
		name = c3rd_other_events.9.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.9.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "citizen_exemption_from_census_tax"			#Applies to all integrated cultures
			duration = -1
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.9.a.tt2
		set_variable = {
			name = census_exemption_given_recently
			days = 3650
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = government_support_movement
			duration = 1825
		}
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
	}
	option = {
		#take my money and shutup
		name = c3rd_other_events.9.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.9.b.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
				}
			}
			add_stability = 5
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = 2
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = 0
			subtract = root.has_monthly_income
			multiply = 15
		}
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 4
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 4
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 4
			}
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = deflation_value
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = deflation_value
					add = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no way
		name = c3rd_other_events.9.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.9.c.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
				}
			}
			add_stability = -3
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -6
		}
		scope:character_taxed_1 = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:character_taxed_2 = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:character_taxed_3 = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.11 = {
	#new ruler, in case of military anarchy, let's pay high sum of money to keep men loyals
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.11.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.11.desc"
	picture = greek_court
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:general_leader_money
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_land = yes
		has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
		any_character = {
			is_ruler = no
			is_general = yes
			NOT = {
				is_friend = ruler
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_general = yes
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ruler
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = general_leader_money
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					is_general = yes
					is_ruler = no
					NOT = {
						is_friend = ruler
					}
				}
				add_popularity = 15
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.11.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.11.a.tt1
		add_legitimacy = 10
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -25
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_general = yes
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ruler
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = softened
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.11.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.11.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			has_law = monetary_reform_law
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = 10
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silver_unvalue
				has_law = monetary_reform_law
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = silver_unvalue
				add = 1
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_general = yes
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ruler
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = softened
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.11.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.11.c.tt1
		add_legitimacy = -15
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_general = yes
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					is_friend = ruler
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.11.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.11.d.tt1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = military_advantages
			}
		}

	#games
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.12.t"
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = yeah_games
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.12.desc.1"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = yeah_games
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.12.desc.2"
		}
	}
	picture = gladiators
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		invention = public_games
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_variable = did_games
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 70
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 80
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stability >= 90
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 0
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_variable = new_ruler_games
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = did_games
			days = 1825
		}
	}
	option = {
		#great games
		name = c3rd_other_events.12.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.12.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = public_games_modifier
			duration = 1825
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = yeah_games
			}
			add_treasury = {
				value = has_monthly_income
				multiply = -10
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = {
				value = country_population
				multiply = -1
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = 25
	}
	option = {
		#create money
		name = c3rd_other_events.12.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.12.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			has_law = monetary_reform_law
			NOT = {
				has_variable = yeah_games
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = public_games_modifier
			duration = 1825
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -8
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silver_unvalue
				has_law = monetary_reform_law
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = silver_unvalue
				add = 1
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = 10
	}
	option = {
		#little games
		name = c3rd_other_events.12.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.12.c.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = yeah_games
			}
			add_treasury = {
				value = has_monthly_income
				multiply = -2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = {
				value = country_population
				multiply = 0.3
				min = {
					value = num_of_cities
					multiply = 5
				}
				multiply = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no games
		name = c3rd_other_events.12.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.12.d.tt1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = yeah_games
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = no_games_modifier
			duration = 1825
		}
		add_stability = -5
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -20
		}
	}
}

			add_corruption = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.14.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.14.c.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				finesse >= 10
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -20
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.15 = {
	#Solidus 3 : stability of gold
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.15.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.15.desc"
	picture = persepolis
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_office = office_magistrate
					has_office = office_steward
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = office_treasure_man
		}
	}
	option = {
		#pay
		name = c3rd_other_events.15.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.15.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = big_monetary_change
			duration = 1825
		}
	}
	option = {
		#office man take the
		name = c3rd_other_events.15.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.15.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:office_treasure_man
			scope:office_treasure_man = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = intelligent
					has_trait = founder
					has_trait = polymath
					has_trait = scholar
				}
			}
		}
		scope:office_treasure_man = {
			add_corruption = 25
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 5
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ruler too cool
		name = c3rd_other_events.15.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.15.c.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = intelligent
					has_trait = founder
					has_trait = polymath
					has_trait = scholar
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -20
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.16 = {
	#Solidus final
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.16.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.16.desc"
	picture = trade_port
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		change_law = basic_monetary_law
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = deflation_value
			}
			remove_variable = deflation_value
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silver_unvalue
			}
			remove_variable = silver_unvalue
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = monetary_consolidation_sol
			}
			remove_country_modifier = monetary_consolidation_sol
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = small_deflation
			}
			remove_country_modifier = small_deflation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = medium_deflation
			}
			remove_country_modifier = medium_deflation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = high_deflation
			}
			remove_country_modifier = high_deflation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = small_monetary_crash
			}
			remove_country_modifier = small_monetary_crash
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = medium_monetary_crash
			}
			remove_country_modifier = medium_monetary_crash
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
			}
			remove_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
		}
	}
	option = {
		#pay
		name = c3rd_other_events.16.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.16.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = solidus_introduced
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.30 = {
	# slave revolts
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.30.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.30.desc"
	picture = revolt
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_country_culture = {
			has_pop_type_right = slaves
			NOR = {
				has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
				has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
				has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
				has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = culture_slave_check
			root = {
				any_owned_province = {
					count >= 5
					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_check.culture
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				has_country_culture_modifier = integration_status_removed
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				has_country_culture_modifier = nobles_revoked				#because they use the other event
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				has_country_culture_modifier = nobles_revoked
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				country_culture_pop_count >= 500
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				country_culture_pop_count >= 200
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				has_pop_type_right = slaves
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = culture_slave_check
				root = {
					any_owned_province = {
						count >= 5
						dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_check.culture
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					has_country_culture_modifier = integration_status_removed
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					save_temporary_scope_as = culture_slave_check2
					root = {
						any_owned_province = {
							count >= 10
							dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_check2.culture
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					save_temporary_scope_as = culture_slave_check2
					root = {
						any_owned_province = {
							count >= 15
							dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_check2.culture
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					country_culture_pop_count >= 200
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					country_culture_pop_count >= 500
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = culture_slave_revolt
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = max_number_massacre
			value = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
					country_culture_pop_count >= 200
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = max_number_massacre
				add = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
					country_culture_pop_count >= 500
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = max_number_massacre
				add = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no
		name = c3rd_other_events.30.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.30.a.tt1
		scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = on_going_revolt
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#diplo
		name = c3rd_other_events.30.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.30.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
				OR = {
					charisma >= 10
					has_trait = prominent
					has_trait = silver_tongued
					has_trait = orator
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			ordered_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_revolt.culture
				}
				order_by = total_population
				max = var:max_number_massacre
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = local_autonomy_c3rd
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -10
		scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = emancipation_c3rd
				duration = 1850
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#massacre
		name = c3rd_other_events.30.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.30.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = good_natured
					has_trait = merciful
					has_trait = benefactor
				}
				OR = {
					martial >= 10
					has_trait = cruel
					has_trait = energetic
					has_trait = harsh
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			ordered_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_slave_revolt.culture
				}
				order_by = total_population
				max = var:max_number_massacre
				every_pops_in_province = {
					limit = {
						pop_culture = scope:culture_slave_revolt.culture
					}
					random_list = {
						3 = {
						}
						1 = {
							kill_pop = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = slaves_massacre_c3rd
				duration = 1850
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#cede
		name = c3rd_other_events.30.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.30.d.tt1
		add_stability = -3
		scope:culture_slave_revolt = {
			set_country_culture_right = freemen
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = max_number_massacre
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.31 = {
	# slaves culture revolts
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.31.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.31.desc"
	goto_location = scope:new_country_slave
	picture = revolt
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_country_culture = {
			has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
			save_temporary_scope_as = check_culture
			root = {
				any_country_state = {
					count >= 3
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.state
					}
					any_state_province = {
						count >= 2
						dominant_province_culture = scope:check_culture.culture
					}
					OR = {
						any_state_province = {
							state_loyalty <= 30
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 4
							has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 10
				has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 15
				has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 20
				has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 30
				has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 0
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
				save_temporary_scope_as = check_culture2
				root = {
					any_country_state = {
						count >= 3
						NOT = {
							this = root.capital_scope.state
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 2
							dominant_province_culture = scope:check_culture2.culture
						}
						OR = {
							any_state_province = {
								state_loyalty <= 30
							}
							any_state_province = {
								count >= 4
								has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = revolting_slave_culture
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = revolting_slaves_c3rd
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		ordered_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_slave_culture.culture
			}
			order_by = total_population
			max = 1
			save_scope_as = new_country_slave
		}
		scope:revolting_slave_culture = {
			remove_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
		}
	}
	option = {
		#vassal
		name = c3rd_other_events.31.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.31.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = -30
		scope:new_country_slave = {
			create_country = {
				save_scope_as = new_country_vassal
				change_government = despotic_monarchy
				add_treasury = 50
				set_variable = {
					name = recent_client
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		scope:new_country_vassal = {
			add_military_experience_to_new_country_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.state
					}
					any_state_province = {
						count >= 4
						dominant_province_culture = scope:check_culture2.culture
					}
					OR = {
						any_state_province = {
							state_loyalty <= 30
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 4
							has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 5
							dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_slave_culture.culture
						}
					}
				}
				every_state_province = {
					set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_slave_culture.culture
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
			}
		}
		make_subject = {
			target = scope:new_country_vassal
			type = client_state
		}
	}
	option = {
		#war
		name = c3rd_other_events.31.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.31.b.tt1
		add_stability = 5
		scope:new_country_slave = {
			create_country = {
				save_scope_as = new_country_vassal
				change_government = despotic_monarchy
				add_treasury = 50
			}
		}
		scope:new_country_vassal = {
			add_military_experience_to_new_country_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_state = {
				limit = {
					any_state_province = {
						count >= 5
						dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_slave_culture.culture
					}
				}
				every_state_province = {
					set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_slave_culture.culture
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
			}
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					any_governorship_state = {
						any_state_province = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								has_owner = yes
								owner = scope:new_country_vassal
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_governorship_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							any_state_province = {
								state_loyalty <= 20
							}
							any_state_province = {
								count >= 4
								has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
							}
						}
					}
					every_state_province = {
						set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
					}
				}
			}
			every_country_state = {
				limit = {
					any_state_province = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_owner = yes
							owner = scope:new_country_vassal
						}
					}
					OR = {
						any_state_province = {
							state_loyalty <= 20
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 4
							has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
						}
					}
				}
				every_state_province = {
					set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						has_owner = yes
						owner = scope:new_country_vassal
					}
					has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
			}
		}
		declare_war_with_wargoal = {
			war_goal = conquer_wargoal
			province = scope:new_country_vassal.capital_scope
			target = scope:new_country_vassal
		}
		scope:new_country_vassal = {
			every_owned_province = {
				add_claim = root
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.321 = {
	# nobles have lost their rights
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.321.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.321.desc"
	picture = roman_trial
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		NOR = {
			#these are modifiers gained on missions when you cnage primary culture, exception with the modifier gained at this moment is to avoid large revolt of the previous primary culture pops
			has_country_modifier = igk_mission_hybridization_modifier			#hybridization from inv indo-germanic
			has_country_modifier = indoparthia_cmod2			#indopartia mission tree
		}
		any_country_culture = {
			NOT = {
				has_pop_type_right = nobles
			}
			NOR = {
				has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
				has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
				has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
				has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
				has_country_culture_modifier = simili_elite
				has_country_culture_modifier = silver_coins_c3rd
			}
			NOT = {
				#for the big diadochy hellenic culture
				this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:hellenic
				root = {
					has_country_modifier = heirs_of_alexander
				}
			}
			has_country_culture_modifier = nobles_revoked
			save_temporary_scope_as = culture_ex_noble_check
			root = {
				any_owned_province = {
					count >= 5
					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_ex_noble_check.culture
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			#if recently promoted
			factor = 200
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd

					has_pop_type_right = nobles

				NOT = {
					#for the big diadochy hellenic culture
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:hellenic

					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = simili_elite
					has_country_culture_modifier = silver_coins_c3rd
				}
				country_culture_pop_count >= 500
				has_country_culture_modifier = nobles_revoked
				NOT = {
					has_pop_type_right = nobles
				}
				NOT = {
					#for the big diadochy hellenic culture
					this.culture.culture_group = culture_group:hellenic
					root = {
						has_country_modifier = heirs_of_alexander
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_culture = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = emancipation_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = slaves_massacre_c3rd
					has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
					has_country_culture_modifier = simili_elite
					has_country_culture_modifier = silver_coins_c3rd

				scope:culture_ex_noble = {

				}

				add = 10

		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.321.a.tt1

			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = on_going_mass_revolt
				duration = 3650
			}
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = growing_revolt
				duration = 1825
			}
			if = {

					has_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite

			}

					has_pop_type_right = slaves
				}
			}
		}

				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_ex_noble.culture

				max = var:max_number_massacre
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = local_autonomy_nobles_c3rd
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -10
		scope:culture_ex_noble = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = simili_elite
				duration = 1850
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
				}
				remove_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#massacre
		name = c3rd_other_events.321.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.321.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = good_natured

					has_trait = benefactor
				}

					martial >= 10
					has_trait = cruel
					has_trait = energetic
					has_trait = harsh
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_tyranny = 10
		add_stability = -8
		hidden_effect = {
			ordered_owned_province = {

					dominant_province_culture = scope:culture_ex_noble.culture
				}

							kill_pop = yes

					}
				}
			}
		}
		scope:culture_ex_noble = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = slaves_massacre_c3rd
				duration = 1850
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
				}
				remove_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#cede
		name = c3rd_other_events.321.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.321.d.tt1
		add_stability = -5
		scope:culture_ex_noble = {
			set_country_culture_right = nobles
		}
	}
	option = {
		#silver
		name = c3rd_other_events.321.e
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.321.e.tt1
		trigger = {
			has_law = monetary_reform_law
			current_ruler = {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
			}
			scope:culture_ex_noble = {
				NOT = {
					has_pop_type_right = slaves
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = silver_unvalue
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = silver_unvalue
					add = 10
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					name = silver_unvalue
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		scope:culture_ex_noble = {
			add_country_culture_modifier = {
				name = silver_coins_c3rd
				duration = 1850
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
				}
				remove_country_culture_modifier = new_culture_elite
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = max_number_massacre
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.32 = {
	# noble revoked culture revolts
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.32.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.32.desc"
	goto_location = scope:new_country_noble
	picture = revolt
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_country_culture = {
			has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
			NOR = {
				has_country_culture_modifier = growing_revolt
				has_pop_type_right = nobles
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = check_culture
			root = {
				OR = {
					any_country_state = {
						count >= 3
						root = {
							num_of_cities <= 500
						}
						NOT = {
							this = root.capital_scope.state
						}
						has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
					}
					any_country_state = {
						count >= 5
						root = {
							num_of_cities >= 500
						}
						NOT = {
							this = root.capital_scope.state
						}
						has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 5
				root = {
					num_of_cities <= 500
				}
				has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 7
				has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 10
				has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 15
				has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			legitimacy <= 0
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				has_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
				save_temporary_scope_as = check_culture2
				NOT = {
					has_country_culture_modifier = growing_revolt
				}
				root = {
					OR = {
						any_country_state = {
							count >= 3
							root = {
								num_of_cities <= 500
							}
							NOT = {
								this = root.capital_scope.state
							}
							has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
						}
						any_country_state = {
							count >= 5
							root = {
								num_of_cities >= 500
							}
							NOT = {
								this = root.capital_scope.state
							}
							has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = revolting_noble_culture
		}
		ordered_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				this.state = {
					has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
				}
			}
			order_by = total_population
			max = 1
			save_scope_as = new_country_noble
		}
		scope:revolting_noble_culture = {
			remove_country_culture_modifier = on_going_mass_revolt
		}
		scope:new_country_noble = {
			create_country = {
				save_scope_as = new_country_vassal
				change_government = despotic_monarchy
				add_treasury = 50
				set_variable = {
					name = recent_client
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.state
					}
					has_state_modifier = secess_preparation
				}
				every_state_province = {
					set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#vassal
		name = c3rd_other_events.32.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.32.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = -30
		scope:new_country_vassal = {
			add_military_experience_to_new_country_effect = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recent_client
				days = 365
			}
		}
		make_subject = {
			target = scope:new_country_vassal
			type = client_state
		}
	}
	option = {
		#war
		name = c3rd_other_events.32.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.32.b.tt1
		add_stability = 5
		scope:new_country_vassal = {
			add_military_experience_to_new_country_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					dominant_province_culture = scope:revolting_noble_culture.culture
					NOT = {
						this.state = root.capital_scope.state
					}
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
			}
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					any_governorship_state = {
						any_state_province = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								has_owner = yes
								owner = scope:new_country_vassal
							}
							NOT = {
								this.state = root.capital_scope.state
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_governorship_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							any_state_province = {
								state_loyalty <= 20
							}
							any_state_province = {
								count >= 4
								has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							this = root.capital_scope.state
						}
					}
					every_state_province = {
						set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
					}
				}
			}
			every_country_state = {
				limit = {
					any_state_province = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_owner = yes
							owner = scope:new_country_vassal
						}
					}
					OR = {
						any_state_province = {
							state_loyalty <= 20
						}
						any_state_province = {
							count >= 4
							has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.state
					}
				}
				every_state_province = {
					set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
				}
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						has_owner = yes
						owner = scope:new_country_vassal
					}
					has_province_modifier = revolt_preparation
					NOT = {
						this.state = root.capital_scope.state
					}
				}
				set_owned_by = scope:new_country_vassal
			}
			scope:new_country_vassal = {
				every_owned_province = {
					add_claim = root
				}
			}
		}
		declare_war_with_wargoal = {
			war_goal = conquer_wargoal
			province = scope:new_country_vassal.capital_scope
			target = scope:new_country_vassal
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.33 = {
	#new cultural identity
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.33.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.33.desc"
	picture = city_country
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		current_date >= 950.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		random_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					this.culture = root.culture
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = checktempculture1
				root = {
					capital_scope = {
						state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_pops_in_province = {
									pop_culture = scope:checktempculture1.culture
								}
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						any_country = {
							rank = great_power
							NOT = {
								this = root
							}
							primary_culture = scope:checktempculture1.culture
						}
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = country_culture_pop_count
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					root = {
						country_culture_group = prev.culture.culture_group
					}
					any_country = {
						rank = great_power
						NOT = {
							this = root
						}
						country_culture_group = prev.culture.culture_group
						NOT = {
							capital_scope.region = {
								any_neighbor_region = {
									any_neighbor_region = {
										any_neighbor_region = {
											this = root.capital_scope.region
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = new_cultural_identity
		}
		random_country_culture = {
			limit = {
				this.culture = root.culture
			}
			save_scope_as = old_culture_scope
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = nope_not_this_culture
			days = 7300
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let's go, new culture and bonuses
		name = c3rd_other_events.33.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.33.a.tt1
		set_primary_culture = scope:new_cultural_identity.culture
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = new_beginnings_mod
			duration = 18500
		}
	}
	option = {
		#oooops no ai should not choose this anyway
		name = c3rd_other_events.33.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.33.b.tt1
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = new_beginnings_mod
				}
				scope:old_culture_scope = {
					add_country_culture_modifier = {
						name = "new_beginnings_c3rd"
						duration = 7300						#20 years
					}
					set_country_culture_right = nobles
					add_integration_progress = 1
					remove_country_culture_modifier = integration_status_removed
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_culture_modifier = too_many_foreigners
						}
						remove_country_culture_modifier = too_many_foreigners
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.40 = {
	#corruption from gold -- MODIFIED now it looks for head_intent_consolidate and propose you to pay people more
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.40.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.40.desc"
	right_portrait = scope:first_consolidate_more_gold
	right_portrait = scope:second_consolidate_more_gold
	picture = greek_court
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 600.1.1
		treasury >= 10000
		has_civil_war = no
		OR = {
			treasury >= income_150
			treasury >= 90000
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = got_chest_open
		}
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
		}
		#part solidus
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		any_character = {
			has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
			is_ruler = no
		}
		any_character = {
			count >= 2
			is_ruler = no
			OR = {
				has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
				AND = {
					has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
					root = {
						towards_civil_war = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			treasury >= income_300
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			current_ruler = {
				has_trait = honest
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			current_ruler = {
				has_trait = righteous
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = got_chest_open
			days = 9125
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = has_economic_reforms_variable
			days = 19000
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
			}
			save_scope_as = first_consolidate_more_gold
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					this = scope:first_consolidate_more_gold
				}
				OR = {
					has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					AND = {
						has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
						root = {
							towards_civil_war = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_consolidate_more_gold
		}
	}
	option = {
		#more 
		name = c3rd_other_events.40.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.40.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_any_office = yes
						has_tech_office = yes
						is_governor = yes
						is_ruler = yes
						is_co_ruler = yes
					}
				}
				add_corruption = 10
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = more_gold_for_peoples
			duration = 18250
		}
	}
	option = {
		#nope, they'll serve themselves
		name = c3rd_other_events.40.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.40.b.tt1
		add_political_influence = -10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = more_gold_help_yourself
			duration = 18250
		}
	}
	option = {
		#mine mine !
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_country_modifier = political_turmoils
				has_country_modifier = political_unstability
				scope:first_consolidate_more_gold = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				}
				scope:second_consolidate_more_gold = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				}
			}
		}
		name = c3rd_other_events.40.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.40.c.tt1
		add_tyranny = 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 80
			}
			add_stability = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 70
			}
			add_stability = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 60
			}
			add_stability = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 50
			}
			add_stability = -5
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -3
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.41 = {
	#corruption from gold -- the military now wants more

		}

					}

			days = 18000
		}

			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
			}
			save_scope_as = first_consolidate_more_gold
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					this = scope:first_consolidate_more_gold
				}
				OR = {
					has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					AND = {
						has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
						root = {
							towards_civil_war = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_consolidate_more_gold
		}
	}
	option = {
		#more 
		name = c3rd_other_events.41.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = yes
						is_ruler = yes
						is_co_ruler = yes
					}
				}
				add_corruption = 10
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.a.tt2
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			}

				name = more_gold_for_military
				duration = 18250
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = more_gold_help_mil
				duration = 18250
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#nope, they'll serve themselves
		name = c3rd_other_events.41.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.b.tt1
		add_political_influence = -10
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.a.tt2
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = more_gold_for_military_2
				duration = 18250
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = more_gold_help_mil_2
				duration = 18250
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#mine mine !
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_country_modifier = political_turmoils
				has_country_modifier = political_unstability
				has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
				scope:first_consolidate_more_gold = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				}
				scope:second_consolidate_more_gold = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				}
			}
		}
		name = c3rd_other_events.41.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.c.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = basic_administrative_law
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.41.c.tt2
			add_legitimacy = -10
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					is_general = yes
					is_ruler = no
					is_mercenary = no
				}
				add_loyalty = disappointed
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = unworthy_leader
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = unworthy_leader
					add = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					name = unworthy_leader
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tyranny = 10
			add_political_influence = -25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 80
			}
			add_stability = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 70
			}
			add_stability = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 60
			}
			add_stability = -8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				stability >= 50
			}
			add_stability = -5
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -3
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.42 = {
	#corruption from gold -- renewal
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.42.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.42.desc"
	right_portrait = scope:first_consolidate_more_gold_soldier
	right_portrait = scope:second_consolidate_more_gold_soldier
	picture = greek_court
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 600.1.1
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military_2
			has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil_2
		}
		NOR = {
			has_variable = got_chest_open_2
			has_variable = got_chest_open
			has_variable = has_economic_reforms_variable
		}
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#yes keep it
		name = c3rd_other_events.42.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.42.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = 25
		add_stability = 5
		set_variable = {
			name = has_economic_reforms_variable
			days = 18000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_for_peoples
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = more_gold_for_peoples
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {

					days = 9125

			else_if = {

					has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_help_yourself

					name = more_gold_help_yourself
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = got_chest_open
					days = 9125
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = more_gold_for_military
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = got_chest_open_2
					days = 9125
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = more_gold_help_mil
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = got_chest_open_2
					days = 9125
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military_2
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_for_military_2
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = more_gold_for_military_2
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = got_chest_open_2
					days = 9125
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil_2
				}
				remove_country_modifier = more_gold_help_mil_2
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = more_gold_help_mil_2
					duration = 18250
				}
				set_variable = {
					name = got_chest_open_2
					days = 9125
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#nope, no more 
		name = c3rd_other_events.42.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.42.b.tt1
		set_variable = {
			name = got_chest_open
			days = 9125
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = got_chest_open_2
			days = 9125
		}

			add_political_influence = -50

				limit = {
					stability >= 80
				}

			}

				}
				add_stability = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					stability >= 60
				}
				add_stability = -5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					stability >= 50
				}
				add_stability = -3
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -2
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_influence = -25
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				OR = {
					has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.50 = {
	#Great work gets pillaged by starving people
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.50.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.50.desc"
	goto_location = scope:wonder_province_starve
	picture = great_work_riot
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		any_owned_province = {
			has_great_work = yes
			NOR = {
				has_variable = wonder_food_given
				has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
			}
			unrest_in_province_svalue >= 5
			state = {
				has_state_food = 0
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = wonder_food_problem
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability <= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 3
				has_great_work = yes
				NOR = {
					has_variable = wonder_food_given
					has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				}
				unrest_in_province_svalue >= 5
				state = {
					has_state_food = 0
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 5
				has_great_work = yes
				NOR = {
					has_variable = wonder_food_given
					has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				}
				unrest_in_province_svalue >= 5
				state = {
					has_state_food = 0
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_owned_province = {
				count >= 8
				has_great_work = yes
				NOR = {
					has_variable = wonder_food_given
					has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				}
				unrest_in_province_svalue >= 5
				state = {
					has_state_food = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_great_work = yes
				NOR = {
					has_variable = wonder_food_given
					has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				}
				state = {
					has_state_food = 0
				}
				unrest_in_province_svalue >= 5
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = total_population
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = wonder_province_starve
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = wonder_food_problem
			days = 365
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = manpower_number
			value = scope:wonder_province_starve.total_population
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = manpower_number
			multiply = 3
		}
	}
	option = {
		#give them food
		name = c3rd_other_events.50.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.50.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				state = {
					has_state_food > 300
				}
			}
		}
		random_country_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_food > 300
			}
			add_state_food = -200
			save_temporary_scope_as = that_province_food
		}
		add_political_influence = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -20
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = 10
			min = {
				value = scope:wonder_province_starve.total_population
				multiply = 20
			}
			multiply = -1
		}
		scope:wonder_province_starve = {
			set_variable = {
				name = wonder_food_given
				days = 1850
			}
			state = {
				add_state_food = 200
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#give them sword
		name = c3rd_other_events.50.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.50.b.tt1
		add_political_influence = -20
		if = {
			limit = {
				manpower < var:manpower_number
			}
			add_stability = -10
		}
		add_manpower = {
			value = scope:wonder_province_starve.total_population
			multiply = -3
		}
		scope:wonder_province_starve = {
			set_variable = {
				name = wonder_food_given
				days = 1850
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = wonder_defended_weapons
					}
					remove_province_modifier = wonder_defended_weapons
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wonder_defended_weapons
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#do not move
		name = c3rd_other_events.50.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.50.c.tt1
		scope:wonder_province_starve = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = manpower_number
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.51 = {
	#Great work restaured
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.51.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.51.desc"
	picture = great_work_architect
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		any_owned_province = {
			has_great_work = yes
			has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_great_work = yes
				has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = total_population
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = wonder_province_destroyed_1
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_great_work = yes
				has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				NOT = {
					this = scope:wonder_province_destroyed_1

				modifier = {
					add = total_population
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = wonder_province_destroyed_2
		}

			limit = {
				has_great_work = yes
				has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
				NOR = {

					this = scope:wonder_province_destroyed_2

					add = total_population
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = wonder_province_destroyed_3

			multiply = -5
		}
		add_political_influence = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
		}
		scope:wonder_province_destroyed_1 = {
			remove_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
			set_variable = {
				name = wonder_food_problem
				days = 10000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#repair choice 2

		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.51.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:wonder_province_destroyed_2 = {
				has_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier
			}
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = num_of_cities
			multiply = -5
		}
		add_political_influence = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
		}
		scope:wonder_province_destroyed_2 = {
			remove_province_modifier = wonder_destroyed_modifier

				days = 10000
			}

	}
	option = {

		}
		not = {
