		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 70
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 80
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 90
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 10
				has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 15
				has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_country_state = {
				count >= 20
				has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_cities >= 500
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_cities >= 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_cities >= 2000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_cities >= 3000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			num_of_cities >= 4000
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = barbarian_border_stabhit
			days = 1850
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities <= 500
			}
			add_stability = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities <= 1000
			}
			add_stability = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities <= 2000
			}
			add_stability = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities <= 3000
			}
			add_stability = -15
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -20
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -10
		}
		if = {
			#the owner is the ruler
			limit = {
				any_governorships = {
					count >= 6
					any_governorship_state = {
						has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
					}
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = root.current_ruler
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.60.desc.tt1
			add_legitimacy = -30
			add_stability = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_governorships = {
					count >= 3
					any_governorship_state = {
						has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
					}
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = root.current_ruler
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.60.desc.tt1
			add_legitimacy = -20
			add_stability = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_governorships = {
					count >= 1
					any_governorship_state = {
						has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
					}
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = root.current_ruler
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.60.desc.tt1
			add_legitimacy = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#legitimacy cost
		name = c3rd_other_events.60.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.60.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			is_monarchy = yes
		}
		add_legitimacy = -30
	}
	option = {
		#governors
		name = c3rd_other_events.60.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.60.b.tt1
		every_governorships = {
			limit = {
				any_governorship_state = {
					has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
				}
			}
			governor = {
				add_loyalty = governor_abandonned
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						#if not already milanarch
						has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						has_variable = recent_military_anarchy
						has_variable = on_going_rep_thingy
						has_country_modifier = political_unstability
					}
					has_variable = unworthy_leader
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						modifier = {
							add = 10
							var:unworthy_leader <= 2
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 10
							NOT = {
								has_variable = unworthy_leader
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							legitimacy >= 85
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 10
							has_law = constantine_reform_law
						}
						modifier = {
							#decentralized administration means the governor will take measures
							add = 12
							has_law = decentralized_administration_law
						}
					}
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							add = var:unworthy_leader
							has_variable = unworthy_leader
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							legitimacy < 50
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							legitimacy < 25
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							legitimacy < 0
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							stability < 25
						}
						trigger_event = {
							id = c3rd_events.9
							days = 15
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_law = decentralized_administration_law
						any_governorships = {
							any_governorship_state = {
								has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
								any_state_province = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										NOT = {
											owner = root
										}
									}
								}
							}
							has_variable = governorship_owner
						}
					}
				}
				random_governorships = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = governorship_owner
								NOT = {
									var:governorship_owner = root.current_ruler
								}
							}
							root = {
								has_law = decentralized_administration_law
							}
						}
						any_governorship_state = {
							has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									NOT = {
										owner = root
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							root = {
								has_law = decentralized_administration_law
							}
						}
						governor = {
							save_scope_as = duchy_creator
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_variable = governorship_owner
						}
						var:governorship_owner = {
							save_scope_as = duchy_creator
						}
					}
					random_governorship_state = {
						limit = {
							has_state_modifier = barbarians_border
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									NOT = {
										owner = root
									}
								}
							}
						}
						random_state_province = {
							weight = {
								modifier = {
									add = total_population
								}
							}
							save_scope_as = duchy_capital
						}
					}
				}
				create_duchy = yes
				trigger_event = {
					id = c3rd_other_events.104
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#events when in the mud
c3rd_other_events.70 = {
	#aristocracy acts against deflation
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.70.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.70.desc"
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = deflation_value
		has_country_modifier = high_deflation
		NOR = {
			has_variable = aristocrats_deflation
			has_country_modifier = aristocratic_reforms
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability < 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability < 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability < 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = deflation_value
			var:deflation_value >= 150
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = deflation_value
			var:deflation_value >= 175
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = deflation_value
			var:deflation_value >= 200
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = aristocrats_deflation
			days = 3650
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let them do
		name = c3rd_other_events.70.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.70.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = aristocratic_reforms
			duration = 3650
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = -30
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = 10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = -30
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#seize their assets
		name = c3rd_other_events.70.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.70.b.tt1
		add_tyranny = 10
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				wealth >= 1000
				is_ruler = no
			}
			add_gold = -1000
			add_loyalty = assets_seized
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = populares_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = populares_party
				value = 10
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = optimates_party
				value = -30
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = democratic_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = democratic_party
				value = 10
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = oligarchic_party
				value = -30
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = deflation_value
			add = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#stop them, nothing will be done
		name = c3rd_other_events.70.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.70.c.tt1
		add_stability = -5
		add_political_influence = -15
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				wealth >= 100
				is_ruler = no
			}
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = boni_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = boni_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = traditionalist_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = traditionalist_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.71 = {
	#people revolt against the crash of currency - negative event when currency collapse
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.71.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.71.desc"
	picture = revolt
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = silver_unvalue
		has_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
		num_of_cities >= 400		#to leave a small buffer between 500 and 400 where you don't have the 500 events, but still can get this one
		NOR = {
			has_variable = revolt_against_crash
			has_country_modifier = raise_of_wages
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 150
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 175
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 200
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = tyranny_of_taxation
				has_variable = forced_decuria
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = revolt_against_crash
			days = 3650
		}
		add_stability = -10		#what do you mean, i want to trigger the collapse ? 
	}
	option = {
		#we need to raise the wages
		name = c3rd_other_events.71.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.71.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = raise_of_wages
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_political_influence = -15
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -30
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = 10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -30
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = 20
			}
		}
		every_country_state = {
			limit = {
				state_freemen >= third_of_state_pop
			}
			random_state_province = {
				add_state_loyalty = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#repression and enslave
		name = c3rd_other_events.71.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.71.b.tt1
		add_tyranny = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = populares_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = populares_party
				value = -30
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = optimates_party
				value = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = democratic_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = democratic_party
				value = -30
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = oligarchic_party
				value = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -10
			}
		}
		every_country_state = {
			limit = {
				state_freemen >= third_of_state_pop
			}
			random_state_province = {
				add_state_loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = silver_unvalue
			add = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ignore them
		name = c3rd_other_events.71.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.71.c.tt1
		add_stability = -5
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = boni_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = boni_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = traditionalist_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = traditionalist_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
	}

c3rd_other_events.72 = {
	#Some possibility to balance the monetary value - this is a positive event where you can bring back the scale for a price
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.72.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.72.desc"
	picture = bakery
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = silver_unvalue
		has_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
		NOR = {
			has_variable = actions_against_silver
			has_country_modifier = bartering_authorised
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability < 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability < 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			stability < 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 150
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 175
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 200
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = actions_against_silver
			days = 7300
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let them barter
		name = c3rd_other_events.72.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.a.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = bartering_authorised
			duration = 7300
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = silver_unvalue
			add = -5
		}
	}
	option = {
		#if you have subjects, instaure money controls on border, clients become tributaries
		name = c3rd_other_events.72.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			any_subject = {
				OR = {
					is_subject_type = client_state
					is_subject_type = satrapy
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
		}
		every_subject = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_subject_type = client_state
					is_subject_type = satrapy
				}
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = chosen_subject
			root = {
				hidden_effect = {
					release_subject = scope:chosen_subject
					make_subject = {
						target = scope:chosen_subject
						type = tributary
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = subject_wants_more_cooldown
				}
				remove_variable = subject_wants_more_cooldown
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = subject_wants_more_cooldown
				days = 3650
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = customs_controls
				duration = 3650
			}
			add_truce = {
				target = root
				duration = 1850
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities <= 10
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt2
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -2
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities <= 25
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt2
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -4
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities <= 65
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt3
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -8
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities <= 150
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt3
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -15
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_cities <= 400
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt4
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -25
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.b.tt4
				root = {
					change_variable = {
						name = silver_unvalue
						add = -40
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ignore them
		name = c3rd_other_events.72.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.72.c.tt1
		add_stability = -5
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = boni_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = boni_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = traditionalist_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = traditionalist_party
				value = -10
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.73 = {
	#crash of the currency event : people trying to escape the taxes
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.73.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.73.desc"
	picture = bakery
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = silver_unvalue
		has_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
		num_of_cities >= 400		#to leave a small buffer between 500 and 400 where you don't have the 500 events, but still can get this one
		NOR = {
			has_variable = silver_escape_taxes
			has_variable = forced_decuria
			has_country_modifier = decuria_established
			has_country_modifier = tyranny_of_taxation
			has_country_modifier = escape_silver_taxation
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 150
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 175
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 200
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = silver_escape_taxes
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#reinforce controls and punishments
		name = c3rd_other_events.73.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.73.a.tt1
		add_stability = -2
		add_tyranny = 10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = tyranny_of_taxation
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	option = {
		#establish decuriones
		name = c3rd_other_events.73.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.73.b.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -10
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = decuria_established
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let them
		name = c3rd_other_events.73.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.73.c.tt1
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = escape_silver_taxation
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.74 = {
	#the decuriones are fleeing
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.74.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.74.desc"
	picture = proscription
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_variable = silver_unvalue
		has_country_modifier = high_monetary_crash
		num_of_cities >= 400		#to leave a small buffer between 500 and 400 where you don't have the 500 events, but still can get this one
		has_country_modifier = decuria_established
		NOT = {
			has_variable = forced_decuria
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 150
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 175
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_variable = silver_unvalue
			var:silver_unvalue >= 200
		}
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#reinforce controls and punishments
		name = c3rd_other_events.74.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.74.a.tt1
		add_stability = -2
		add_tyranny = 5
		set_variable = {
			name = forced_decuria
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let them go
		name = c3rd_other_events.74.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.74.b.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -20
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = populares_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = optimates_party
				value = -35
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = democratic_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = oligarchic_party
				value = -35
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = decuria_established
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.75 = {
	#new currency, but the leader is really bad at that
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.75.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.75.desc"
	picture = hellenic_marketplace
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		num_of_cities >= 400		#to leave a small buffer between 500 and 400 where you don't have the 500 events, but still can get this one
		current_ruler = {
			finesse <= 2
			NOT = {
				has_variable = treasureman_fixed_money
			}
		}
		has_variable = silver_unvalue
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_office = office_magistrate
					has_office = office_steward
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = office_treasure_man
		}
	}
	option = {
		#destroy the surplux of cardboard money
		name = c3rd_other_events.75.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.75.a.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = populares_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = boni_party
				value = -20
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
				has_party_type = democratic_party
			}
			add_party_approval = {
				party_type = traditionalist_party
				value = -20
			}
		}
		add_stability = -5
		current_ruler = {
			set_variable = {
				name = treasureman_fixed_money
			}
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -8
		}
	}
	option = {
		#office treasureman is competent enough
		name = c3rd_other_events.75.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.75.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:office_treasure_man
			scope:office_treasure_man = {
				finesse >= 10
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_political_influence = -10
		current_ruler = {
			set_variable = {
				name = treasureman_fixed_money
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#do nothing
		name = c3rd_other_events.75.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.75.c.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -20
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		change_variable = {
			name = silver_unvalue
			add = 25
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.76 = {
	#split the empire
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.76.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.76.desc"
	picture = hellenic_marketplace
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		num_of_cities >= 500
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = p:1453
			}
			p:1453 = {
				save_scope_as = byzantium
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				dominant_province_culture = root.culture
				governorship = {
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.governorship
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = total_population
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					has_province_rank = city
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
					has_province_rank = city_metropolis
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.01
					region = {
						any_neighbor_region = {
							any_region_province = {
								owner = root
								this = root.capital_scope
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value < 600
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 900
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 1200
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = first_split_capital
			governorship = {
				save_scope_as = first_split_govship
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				dominant_province_culture = root.culture
				NOT = {
					this = scope:first_split_capital
				}
				governorship = {
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.governorship
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = total_population
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					has_province_rank = city
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
					has_province_rank = city_metropolis
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.01
					region = {
						any_neighbor_region = {
							any_region_province = {
								owner = root
								this = root.capital_scope
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value < 600
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = scope:first_split_capital
						value < 500
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 900
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 1200
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_split_capital
			governorship = {
				save_scope_as = second_split_govship
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					this = scope:first_split_capital
					this = scope:second_split_capital
				}
				dominant_province_culture = root.culture
				governorship = {
					NOT = {
						this = root.capital_scope.governorship
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = total_population
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					has_province_rank = city
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 100
					has_province_rank = city_metropolis
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.01
					region = {
						any_neighbor_region = {
							any_region_province = {
								owner = root
								this = root.capital_scope
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value < 600
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = scope:first_split_capital
						value < 500
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					distance_from = {
						province = scope:second_split_capital
						value < 500
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 900
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					distance_from = {
						province = root.capital_scope
						value > 1200
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = third_split_capital
			governorship = {
				save_scope_as = third_split_govship
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#choice 1
		name = c3rd_other_events.76.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.a.tt1
		add_stability = 20
		scope:first_split_capital = {
			save_scope_as = split_empire_capital
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = divided_empire
			duration = 18250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.ttm2
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.ttm
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = deflation_value
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.ttd
			change_variable = {
				name = deflation_value
				divide = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = silver_unvalue
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.tts
			change_variable = {
				name = silver_unvalue
				divide = 2
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.ttlag
	}
	option = {
		#choice2
		name = c3rd_other_events.76.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.b.tt1
		add_stability = 20
		scope:second_split_capital = {
			save_scope_as = split_empire_capital
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = divided_empire
			duration = 18250
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.ttm2

				name = deflation_value

			}

			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.tts

		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.76.c.tt1
		add_stability = 20

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}

c3rd_other_events.77 = {
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.77.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.77.desc"
	picture = ship_in_storm
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.77.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.77.a.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:split_empire_capital
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				create_split = yes
			}
		}
		every_governorships = {
			limit = {
				is_in_list = old_empire
			}
			remove_from_list = old_empire
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.77.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.77.b.tt1
		every_governorships = {
			limit = {
				is_in_list = old_empire
			}
			remove_from_list = old_empire
		}
	}
}

### ADMINISTRATIVE EVENTS ####
### Basically nobles (great families) taking more power in the realm
### Nothing will almost ever happen as long as you don't reform the administrative law, or enact the Solidus
### Constantine reform is cool because it reduce military anarchy, however it will progressively give power to the governors
### Everything will although stay minor UNTIL you enact Solidus - and then things will snowball
### Solidus is really great because it delete all the monetary crisis mechanics so you don't have to deal with that anymore, but with a secondary effect.
### Those Administrative things are the secondary effect
c3rd_other_events.80 = {
	#Notification of governorship taken by family
	type = minor_country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.80.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.80.desc"
	interface_lock = no
	left_portrait = scope:autonomy_governorship.var:governorship_owner
	trigger = {
		current_date > 750.1.1
		scope:autonomy_governorship = {
			exists = governor
			governor = {
				is_ruler = no
			}
			NOR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = {
						is_head_of_family = yes
						family = scope:autonomy_governorship.governor.family
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = governor
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					region_control_value >= 30
					root = {
						has_law = decentralized_administration_law
					}
				}
				AND = {
					region_control_value >= 40
					root = {
						has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
					}
				}
				region_control_value >= 50
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		scope:autonomy_governorship = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				var:governorship_owner = {
					save_scope_as = ex_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
				scope:ex_owner = {
					recalculate_ownership_char = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = governorship_owner
				value = governor
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
			set_variable = {
				#equivalent à appeler calculate_the_gov_ownership = yes
				name = governorship_owner_ratio
				value = region_control_value				#prend le gov alors que calculate_the_gov_ownership prend le owner, ce qui est la même chose ici
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				governor = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_variable = country_ownership
						}
						remove_variable = country_ownership
					}
					save_scope_as = influent_character
					set_variable = {
						name = country_ownership
						value = country_region_control
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_region_control >= 20
							NOT = {
								has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
							}
						}
						add_character_modifier = {
							name = major_influence_aristocrat
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
							country_region_control < 15
						}
						remove_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "c3rd_other_events.80.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:influent_character = {
					is_minor_character = no
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.80.a.tt1
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.80.a.tt2
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.802 = {
	#Notification of country control ######  FOR DEBUG PURPOSES
	type = minor_country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.80.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.802.desc"
	interface_lock = no
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	trigger = {
		current_date > 750.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = country_ownership
			}
			save_scope_as = owner_target_for_number
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "c3rd_other_events.80.a"
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.75.c.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.81 = {
	#succession ownership
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		is_minor_character = no
		exists = family
		exists = family.head_of_family
		NOT = {
			root = family.head_of_family
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				employer = {
					any_governorships = {
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = root
					}
				}
			}
			family.head_of_family = {
				save_scope_as = ownership_target
			}
			employer = {
				every_governorships = {
					limit = {
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = root
					}
					remove_variable = governorship_owner
					set_variable = {
						name = governorship_owner
						value = scope:ownership_target
					}
					calculate_the_gov_ownership = yes
				}
			}
			scope:ownership_target = {
				recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = country_ownership
				}
				remove_variable = country_ownership
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.811 = {
	#succession ownership
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		is_minor_character = no
		exists = family
		exists = family.head_of_family
		NOT = {
			root = family.head_of_family
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					var:owner_from_another_empire = root
				}
			}
			family.head_of_family = {
				save_scope_as = ownership_target
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					var:owner_from_another_empire = root
				}
				remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
				set_variable = {
					name = owner_from_another_empire
					value = scope:ownership_target
				}
			}
			scope:ownership_target = {
				recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = country_ownership
				}
				remove_variable = country_ownership
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.82 = {
	#take lands from landowner
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.82.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.82.desc"
	picture = hellenic_marketplace
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		exists = scope:target
	}
	immediate = {
		random_governorships = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				var:governorship_owner = scope:target
				save_temporary_scope_as = govtmp_parse
				OR = {
					scope:target = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
					scope:target.family.head_of_family = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
					add = var:governorship_owner_ratio
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = governorship_1
		}
		random_governorships = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				NOT = {
					this = scope:governorship_1
				}
				var:governorship_owner = scope:target
				save_temporary_scope_as = govtmp_parse
				OR = {
					scope:target = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
					scope:target.family.head_of_family = {

					}

			limit = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				NOR = {
					this = scope:governorship_1
					trigger_if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:governorship_2
						}
						this = scope:governorship_2
					}
				}
				var:governorship_owner = scope:target
				save_temporary_scope_as = govtmp_parse
				OR = {
					scope:target = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
					scope:target.family.head_of_family = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5

						}
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
					add = var:governorship_owner_ratio
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = governorship_3
		}
		random_governorships = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				NOR = {
					this = scope:governorship_1
					trigger_if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:governorship_2
						}
						this = scope:governorship_2
					}
					trigger_if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:governorship_3
						}
						this = scope:governorship_3
					}
				}
				var:governorship_owner = scope:target
				save_temporary_scope_as = govtmp_parse
				OR = {
					scope:target = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
					scope:target.family.head_of_family = {
						any_holdings = {
							count >= 5
							governorship = scope:govtmp_parse
						}
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
					add = var:governorship_owner_ratio
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = governorship_4
		}
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = c3rd_other_events.82.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.82.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:governorship_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					is_head_of_family = yes
				}
			}
			scope:target = {
				add_loyalty = property_seized
			}
			add_political_influence = -10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					is_minor_character = no
				}
			}
			scope:target = {
				add_loyalty = property_seized
			}
			scope:target.family.head_of_family = {
				add_loyalty = property_seized_small
			}
			add_political_influence = -5
		}
		else = {
			scope:target = {
				add_loyalty = property_seized
			}
			add_tyranny = 1
			add_political_influence = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
		}
		while = {
			count = 5
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					governorship = scope:governorship_1
					exists = holding_owner
					OR = {
						holding_owner = scope:target
						holding_owner = scope:target.family.head_of_family
					}
				}
				holding_owner = {
					remove_holding = prev
				}
			}
		}
		scope:target = {
			set_variable = {
				name = land_taken_recently
				days = 365
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:governorship_1 = {
				calculate_the_gov_ownership = yes
			}
		}
	}

c3rd_other_events.83 = {
	#Retake governorship failed :  you'll have to negociate
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.83.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.83.desc"
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		exists = scope:regaining_governorship
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			has_variable = governorship_owner
			var:governorship_owner = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#the golden way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt1
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = count_reclaim
			multiply = -1
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			var:governorship_owner = {
				add_gold = {
					value = root.has_monthly_income
					multiply = 3
				}
				add_corruption = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
	option = {
		#the concessions way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.b.tt1
		while = {
			count = count_reclaim
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = no
					NOR = {
						governorship = scope:regaining_governorship
						exists = holding_owner
					}
				}
				weight = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 10
						any_neighbor_province = {
							exists = holding_owner
							holding_owner = scope:regaining_governorship.var:governorship_owner
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 5
						exists = governor
						governor = scope:regaining_governorship.var:governorship_owner
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = holding_target
			}
			scope:regaining_governorship.var:governorship_owner = {
				add_holding = scope:holding_target
			}
		}
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			var:governorship_owner = {
				add_loyalty = traded_holding
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recently_lost_control
				days = 1825				#5years
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
	option = {
		#the hard way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.c.tt1
		add_tyranny = count_reclaim
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			var:governorship_owner = {
				add_loyalty = lost_gov_ownership
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recently_lost_control
				days = 1825				#5years
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
	option = {
		#the smart way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.d.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = intelligent
					has_trait = polymath
					has_trait = obsessive
				}
				finesse >= 8
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = political_influence_reclaim
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recently_lost_control
				days = 1825				#5years
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
	option = {
		#the charismatic way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.e
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.e.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = assertive
					has_trait = prominent
					has_trait = shrewd
					has_trait = silver_tongued
				}
				charisma >= 8
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -15
		}
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			var:governorship_owner = {
				add_popularity = 25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recently_lost_control
				days = 1825				#5years
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
	option = {
		#the blackmail way
		name = c3rd_other_events.83.f
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.f.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = crafty
					has_trait = cruel
					has_trait = tactician
					has_trait = aggressive
				}
				martial >= 8
			}
		}
		add_tyranny = 4
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -5
		}
		scope:regaining_governorship = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
				}
				remove_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
			}
		}
		scope:ex_owner_calc_purp = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
			set_variable = {
				name = recently_lost_control
				days = 1825				#5years
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.83.a.tt2
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.84 = {
	#event when you have  the tax inspection culture law : great nobles invest in land
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.84.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.84.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = indian_city
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		has_country_modifier = tax_inspection
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_character = {
			count > 2
			loyalty <= 50
			is_head_of_family = yes
			is_ruler = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = had_land_tax_evasion
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			stability >= 70
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stability >= 90
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			current_ruler = {
				corruption >= 25
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			current_ruler = {
				corruption >= 50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			treasury >= 60000
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = had_land_tax_evasion
			days = 10000			#27 years
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					governor = {
						is_ruler = no
						OR = {
							corruption >= 30
							loyalty < 50
						}
					}
					any_governorship_state = {
						any_state_province = {
							NOT = {
								exists = holding_owner
							}
						}
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = governorship_parse
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							governorship = scope:governorship_parse
							NOT = {
								exists = holding_owner
							}
						}
						save_scope_as = holding_target
						governor = {
							add_holding = scope:holding_target
							add_corruption = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let it go
		name = c3rd_other_events.84.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.84.a.tt1
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				is_ruler = no
			}
			add_loyalty = is_tax_evading
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = land_tax_evasion_authorized
			days = 9000			#24.6 yo
		}
	}
	option = {
		#stop this evasion
		name = c3rd_other_events.84.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.84.b.tt1
		add_tyranny = 6
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				is_ruler = no
			}
			add_loyalty = cant_tax_evading
		}
	}
	option = {
		#offer to reverse the law
		name = c3rd_other_events.84.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.84.c.tt1
		add_political_influence = 10
		remove_country_modifier = tax_inspection
		set_variable = {
			name = tax_inspection_stopped
			days = 3650
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.85 = {
	#You chose your demands, then the landowner answer 5 days later. Everything is determined through variables defined here :
	#landowner_demands : variable that count how powerful and demanding the character will be
	#what_are_we_asking : variable to track what we are asking
	#answer_landowner : variable that define what the landowner will ask (or refuse)
	# all those are deleted once the event 86 is finished
	# the desc and choices and effects of event 86 are determined by the variables, so everything will be in 86
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.85.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.85.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:target
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		scope:target = {
			is_alive = yes
			is_ruler = no
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			#calculation of the landowner's power : 0-2 = weak ; 3-5 = powerful ; 6+ = omnipotent 
			name = landowner_demands
			value = 0
		}
		scope:target = {
			set_variable = {
				name = got_negociated_recently
				days = 1800
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					var:country_ownership >= 20
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					var:country_ownership >= 35
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					var:country_ownership >= 45
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					var:country_ownership >= 60
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					var:country_ownership >= 75
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					power_base >= 30
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					power_base >= 50
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					power_base >= 70
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					corruption >= 50
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = crafty
						has_trait = prominent
						has_trait = assertive
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		scope:target = {
			save_scope_as = asked_landowner
		}
	}
	#what do we want ?
	option = {
		#decrease his power/ownership
		name = c3rd_other_events.85.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			any_governorships = {
				count >= 2
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				var:governorship_owner = scope:target
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					is_disloyal = yes
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = what_are_we_asking
			value = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		#increase his undying loyalty
		name = c3rd_other_events.85.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			towards_civil_war = no
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = what_are_we_asking
			value = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		#ask for bonuses
		name = c3rd_other_events.85.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:target = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = got_extract_more
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = what_are_we_asking
			value = 3
		}
	}
	option = {
		#save the country from civil war !
		name = c3rd_other_events.85.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.d.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:target = {
					is_disloyal = yes
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = landowner_demands
				add = 1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = what_are_we_asking
			value = 4
		}
	}
	option = {
		#cancel
		name = c3rd_other_events.85.e
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.e.tt1
		remove_variable = landowner_demands
	}
	after = {
		#5 days later, the answer
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = what_are_we_asking
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.85.desc2
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						#refuse
						modifier = {
							add = 10
							scope:target = {
								loyalty < 33
							}
							var:what_are_we_asking = 1
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 14
							scope:target = {
								loyalty < 33
							}
							var:what_are_we_asking = 3
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = abrasive
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = suspicious
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = benefactor
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							name = answer_landowner
							value = 1
						}
					}
					4 = {
						#demand political power (chances to coup)
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = ambitious
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = cautious
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = crafty
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							scope:target = {
								var:country_ownership >= 60
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							scope:target = {
								loyalty < 33
							}
							var:what_are_we_asking = 4
						}
						modifier = {
							#already have the modifier
							factor = 0.3
							scope:target = {
								has_character_modifier = political_power_character
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							name = answer_landowner
							value = 2
						}
					}
					5 = {
						#demand independant domain
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = corrupt
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = founder
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = selfish
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.5
							num_of_cities >= 1000
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.5
							num_of_cities >= 2000
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							num_of_cities >= 5000
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.2
							any_governorships = {
								count < country_gov_ratio_number
								has_variable = governorship_owner
								var:governorship_owner = scope:target
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							NOT = {
								any_subject = {
									is_subject_type = autonomous_domain
									has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
									var:owner_from_another_empire = scope:target
								}
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							name = answer_landowner
							value = 3
						}
					}
					5 = {
						#demand special laws - right
						modifier = {
							add = 2
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = assertive
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = crafty
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = 1
							scope:target = {
								has_trait = proud
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -1
							has_country_modifier = law_advantages_4
						}
						modifier = {
							add = -3
							has_country_modifier = law_advantages_5
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.1
							has_law = decentralized_administration_law
						}
						set_variable = {
							name = answer_landowner
							value = 4
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = c3rd_other_events.86
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.86 = {
	#answer from landowner
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.86.t"
	desc = {
		#you meet the landowner
		triggered_desc = {
			#weak
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:landowner_demands < 3
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.1"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#strong
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:landowner_demands >= 3
				var:landowner_demands < 6
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.2"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#omnipotent
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:landowner_demands >= 6
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.3"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#dead
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = no
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.4"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#error
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_variable = landowner_demands
					has_variable = answer_landowner
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.5"
		}
		#what he ask of us
		triggered_desc = {
			#he refuses
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 1
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.11"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#political power
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 2
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.12"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#domain
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 3
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.13"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#law and bonuses
			trigger = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 4
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.86.desc.14"
		}
	}
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:asked_landowner
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		#nothing, because the event needs to be triggered for variable cleaning
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					#choose the governorships to be given as domain
					has_variable = answer_landowner
					var:answer_landowner = 3
				}
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					add_gold = 1
				}
				while = {
					count = landowner_asked_ratio_number
					random_governorships = {
						limit = {
							has_variable = governorship_owner
							var:governorship_owner = scope:asked_landowner
							NOT = {
								is_in_list = family_domain_govs
							}
							OR = {
								NOT = {
									exists = governor
								}
								governor = {
									is_ruler = no
								}
							}
						}
						weight = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 10
								any_governorship_state = {
									any_state_province = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											exists = governorship
											governorship = {
												is_in_list = family_domain_govs
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 10
								any_governorship_state = {
									any_state_province = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											exists = owner
											owner = {
												has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
												var:owner_from_another_empire = scope:asked_landowner
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 3
								any_governorship_state = {
									any_state_province = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											has_owner = yes
											NOT = {
												owner = root
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								any_governorship_state = {
									any_state_province = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											exists = governor
											governor = {
												is_ruler = yes
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_list = family_domain_govs
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#accept his offer
		name = c3rd_other_events.86.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			has_variable = answer_landowner
			NOT = {
				var:answer_landowner = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 3
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt13
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					is_in_list = family_domain_govs
				}
				save_scope_as = gov_tooltip
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.a.tt2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				create_domain = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 2
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_influence = -25
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -20
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -10
			}
			give_political_power_modifier = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 4
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			give_law_change_pol = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_1
			reduce_landowner_domain = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_2
			scope:asked_landowner = {
				add_loyalty = loyalty_acquired
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_3
			apply_landowner_bonuses = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 3
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_41
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 6
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_42
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_43
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#offer gold
		name = c3rd_other_events.86.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				finesse >= scope:asked_landowner.finesse
				OR = {
					has_trait = assertive
					AND = {
						has_trait = silver_tongued
						scope:asked_landowner = {
							has_trait = corrupt
						}
					}
				}
			}
			has_variable = answer_landowner
			NOT = {
				var:answer_landowner = 1
			}
		}
		add_treasury = {
			value = has_monthly_income
			multiply = 4
			multiply = var:landowner_demands
			min = has_monthly_income
			multiply = -1
		}
		scope:asked_landowner = {
			add_gold = {
				value = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = var:landowner_demands
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_1
			reduce_landowner_domain = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_2
			scope:asked_landowner = {
				add_loyalty = loyalty_acquired
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_3
			apply_landowner_bonuses = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 3
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_41
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 6
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_42
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_43
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#negociate better - need to be persuasive and the guy to not be mad
		name = c3rd_other_events.86.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.c.tt1
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {
			scope:asked_landowner = {
				NOR = {
					charisma >= 10
					loyalty <= 33
				}
			}
			current_ruler = {
				charisma >= 10
				OR = {
					has_trait = assertive
					has_trait = silver_tongued
					has_trait = deceitful
					has_trait = shrewd
				}
			}
			has_variable = answer_landowner
			NOT = {
				var:answer_landowner = 1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = negociated_better
			days = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 3
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt13
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					is_in_list = family_domain_govs
				}
				save_scope_as = gov_tooltip
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.a.tt2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				create_domain = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 2
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_influence = -15
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -20
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
			give_political_power_modifier = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
				has_variable = answer_landowner
				var:answer_landowner = 4
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					is_alive = yes
				}
			}
			give_law_change_pol = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 1
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_1
			reduce_landowner_domain = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 2
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_2
			scope:asked_landowner = {
				add_loyalty = loyalty_acquired
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 3
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_3
			apply_landowner_bonuses = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:what_are_we_asking = 4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 3
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_42
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention2
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					var:landowner_demands < 6
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_43
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention3
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.tt1_44
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							loyalty <= 33
						}
						add_loyalty = political_intervention4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#say no
		name = c3rd_other_events.86.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.d.tt1
		trigger = {
			has_variable = answer_landowner

	option = {
		#case when he is dead/bug/refuses
		name = c3rd_other_events.86.e
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.86.e.tt1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				scope:asked_landowner = {
					#dead
					is_alive = no
				}
				AND = {
					#refuses
					has_variable = answer_landowner
					var:answer_landowner = 1
				}
				NOR = {
					#bug
					has_variable = landowner_demands
					has_variable = answer_landowner
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = landowner_demands
			}
			remove_variable = landowner_demands
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = answer_landowner
			}
			remove_variable = answer_landowner
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = answer_landowner
			}
			remove_variable = answer_landowner
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = what_are_we_asking
			}
			remove_variable = what_are_we_asking
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = negociated_better
			}
			remove_variable = negociated_better
		}
		every_governorships = {
			limit = {
				is_in_list = family_domain_govs
			}
			remove_from_list = family_domain_govs
		}
		scope:asked_landowner = {
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.87 = {
	#take region from domain
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.87.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.87.desc"
	picture = hellenic_marketplace
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		exists = scope:target
		scope:target.employer = {
			has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		scope:target.employer = {
			var:owner_from_another_empire = {
				save_scope_as = owner_reintegrated
			}
			random_governorships = {
				weight = {
					modifier = {
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = root
								}
							}
						}
						factor = 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = governorship_1
			}
			random_governorships = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						this = scope:governorship_1
					}
				}
				weight = {
					modifier = {
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = root
								}
							}
						}
						factor = 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = governorship_2
			}
			random_governorships = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						this = scope:governorship_1
						this = scope:governorship_2
					}
				}
				weight = {
					modifier = {
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = root
								}
							}
						}
						factor = 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = governorship_3
			}
			random_governorships = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						this = scope:governorship_1
						this = scope:governorship_2
						this = scope:governorship_3
					}
				}
				weight = {
					modifier = {
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = root
								}
							}
						}
						factor = 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = governorship_4
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = c3rd_other_events.87.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.87.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:governorship_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:governorship_1 = {
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {
						limit = {
							owner = scope:target.employer
						}
						set_owned_by = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
		}
		scope:owner_reintegrated = {
			add_loyalty = reintegrated_domain
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = c3rd_other_events.87.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.87.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:governorship_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:governorship_2 = {
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {
						limit = {
							owner = scope:target.employer
						}
						set_owned_by = root
						random_list = {
							2 = {
							}
							1 = {
								modifier = {
									add = 1
									root = {
										has_law = decentralized_administration_law
									}
								}
								scope:owner_reintegrated = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
		}
		scope:owner_reintegrated = {
			add_loyalty = reintegrated_domain
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = c3rd_other_events.87.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.87.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:governorship_3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:governorship_3 = {
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {
						limit = {
							owner = scope:target.employer
						}
						set_owned_by = root
						random_list = {
							2 = {
							}
							1 = {
								modifier = {
									add = 1
									root = {
										has_law = decentralized_administration_law
									}
								}
								scope:owner_reintegrated = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
		}
		scope:owner_reintegrated = {
			add_loyalty = reintegrated_domain
			recalculate_ownership_char = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		#
		name = c3rd_other_events.87.d
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.87.d.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:governorship_4
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:governorship_4 = {
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {
						limit = {
							owner = scope:target.employer
						}
						set_owned_by = root
						random_list = {
							2 = {
							}
							1 = {
								modifier = {
									add = 1
									root = {
										has_law = decentralized_administration_law
									}
								}
								scope:owner_reintegrated = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = -8
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = 3
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -7
