c3rd_other_events.88 = {
	#when one autonomous domain does not have any owner
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.88.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.88.desc"
	goto_location = scope:subject_without_owner.capital_scope
	picture = hellenic_marketplace
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.88.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.88.a.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:subject_without_owner = {
					num_of_cities < 250
				}
			}
			add_stability = -5
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:subject_without_owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					set_owned_by = root
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.88.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.88.b.tt1
		hidden_effect = {
			release_subject = scope:subject_without_owner
			make_subject = {
				target = scope:subject_without_owner
				type = client_state
			}
			scope:subject_without_owner = {
				remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
				set_variable = {
					name = recent_client
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:subject_without_owner = {
					num_of_cities < 250
				}
			}
			add_stability = 5
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = 10
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.89 = {
	#when one autonomous domain have owner in foreign country and no heir have been found
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.89.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.89.desc"
	goto_location = scope:subject_with_foreign_owner.capital_scope
	picture = romans_marching
	trigger = {
		exists = scope:subject_with_foreign_owner
		scope:subject_with_foreign_owner = {
			has_land = yes
			has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
			var:owner_from_another_empire = {
				is_alive = yes
				NOT = {
					employer = root
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		scope:subject_with_foreign_owner = {
			var:owner_from_another_empire = {
				employer = {
					save_scope_as = foreign_pretendant
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#annex the domain - lose some
		name = c3rd_other_events.89.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.89.a.tt1
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:subject_with_foreign_owner = {
				while = {
					count = subject_partition_ratio
					random_country_state = {
						weight = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 30
								any_state_province = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										has_owner = yes
										owner = scope:foreign_pretendant
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.2
								any_state_province = {
									any_neighbor_province = {
										has_owner = yes
										owner = root
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 4
								NOT = {
									any_state_province = {
										any_neighbor_province = {
											has_owner = yes
											owner = root
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						every_state_province = {
							set_owned_by = scope:foreign_pretendant
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					set_owned_by = root
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#client
		name = c3rd_other_events.89.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.89.b.tt1
		hidden_effect = {
			release_subject = scope:subject_with_foreign_owner
			make_subject = {
				target = scope:subject_with_foreign_owner
				type = client_state
			}
			scope:subject_with_foreign_owner = {
				remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
				set_variable = {
					name = recent_client
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.891 = {
	#when one autonomous domain have been set independant for a reason or another and the owner is still here
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.891.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.891.desc"
	goto_location = scope:owner_without_subject.capital_scope
	picture = romans_marching
	trigger = {
		exists = scope:owner_without_subject
		scope:owner_without_subject = {
			has_land = yes
			has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
			var:owner_from_another_empire = {
				is_alive = yes
				employer = root
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				war = yes
			}
			every_current_war = {
				limit = {
					is_war_leader = scope:owner_without_subject
				}
				force_white_peace = THIS
			}
		}
		scope:owner_without_subject = {
			var:owner_from_another_empire = {
				save_scope_as = owner_of_nonsubject
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#reintegrate the domain - low num of cities
		name = c3rd_other_events.891.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.891.a.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:owner_without_subject = {
				subject_third_cities < root.num_of_cities
			}
		}
		add_manpower = {
			value = scope:owner_without_subject.num_of_provinces
			multiply = -1
		}
		make_subject = {
			target = scope:owner_without_subject
			type = autonomous_domain
		}
	}
	option = {
		#reintegrate the domain - high num of cities = client
		name = c3rd_other_events.891.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.891.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:owner_without_subject = {
				subject_third_cities >= root.num_of_cities
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			make_subject = {
				target = scope:owner_without_subject
				type = client_state
			}
			add_truce = {
				target = scope:owner_without_subject
				duration = 3650
			}
			scope:owner_of_nonsubject = {
				remove_all_positions = yes
				move_country = scope:owner_without_subject
				set_home_country = scope:owner_without_subject
				every_child = {
					limit = {
						prisoner = no
					}
					remove_all_positions = yes
					move_country = scope:owner_without_subject
					set_home_country = scope:owner_without_subject
				}
			}
			scope:owner_without_subject = {
				set_as_ruler = scope:owner_of_nonsubject
				set_variable = {
					name = recent_client
					days = 365
				}
				remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
			}
			if = {
				#edges
				limit = {
					any_governorships = {
						OR = {
							NOT = {
								exists = governor
							}
							governor = {
								is_ruler = no
							}
						}
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = scope:owner_of_nonsubject
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = scope:owner_without_subject
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_governorships = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							NOT = {
								exists = governor
							}
							governor = {
								is_ruler = no
							}
						}
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = scope:owner_of_nonsubject
						any_governorship_state = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = scope:owner_without_subject
								}
							}
						}
					}
					every_governorship_state = {
						limit = {
							any_state_province = {
								any_neighbor_province = {
									has_owner = yes
									owner = scope:owner_without_subject
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_list = state_join_domain
					}
				}
				every_country_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_list = state_join_domain
					}
					remove_from_list = state_join_domain
					every_state_province = {
						set_owned_by = scope:owner_without_subject
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#conquer it 
		name = c3rd_other_events.891.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.891.c.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 4
		}
		add_manpower = {
			value = scope:owner_without_subject.num_of_cities
			divide = -2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:owner_without_subject = {
					num_of_cities < 100
				}
			}
			add_stability = -5
			add_tyranny = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:owner_without_subject = {
					num_of_cities < 200
				}
			}
			add_stability = -10
			add_tyranny = 6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:owner_without_subject = {
					num_of_cities < 400
				}
			}
			add_stability = -20
			add_tyranny = 9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:owner_without_subject = {
					num_of_cities < 600
				}
			}
			add_stability = -30
			add_tyranny = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				scope:owner_without_subject = {
					num_of_cities < 1000
				}
			}
			add_stability = -40
			add_tyranny = 16
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -50
			add_tyranny = 20
		}
		scope:owner_of_nonsubject = {
			add_loyalty = reintegrated_domain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:owner_without_subject = {
				remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
				every_owned_province = {
					set_owned_by = root
					random_list = {
						1 = {
						}
						1 = {
							modifier = {
								add = 1
								root = {
									has_law = decentralized_administration_law
								}
							}
							scope:owner_of_nonsubject = {
								add_holding = prev
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.90 = {
	#political powerful character - get influence
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.90.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.90.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:pol_target
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_character = {
			has_character_modifier = political_power_character
			loyalty <= 75
			is_ruler = no
			NOT = {
				has_variable = pol_get
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			tyranny >= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				loyalty <= 75
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					has_variable = pol_get
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = pol_target
			set_variable = {
				name = pol_get
				days = 1500				#4y
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#let him do
		name = c3rd_other_events.90.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.90.a.tt1
		scope:pol_target = {
			add_popularity = 20
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					scope:pol_target = {
						popularity >= 98
					}
				}
				add_legitimacy = -10
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = populares_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = populares_party
					value = -10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = optimates_party
					value = -10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = boni_party
					value = -10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					has_party_type = democratic_party
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = democratic_party
					value = -10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = oligarchic_party
					value = -10
				}
				add_party_approval = {
					party_type = traditionalist_party
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_influence = 10
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -5
		}
	}
	option = {
		#more popularity = he get canceled
		name = c3rd_other_events.90.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.90.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			scope:pol_target = {
				current_ruler = {
					popularity > scope:pol_target.popularity
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_political_influence = -5
		scope:pol_target = {
			add_popularity = -10
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no
		name = c3rd_other_events.90.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.90.c.tt1
		scope:pol_target = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		add_tyranny = 2
		add_political_influence = -5
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.91 = {
	#political powerful character - coup
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.91.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.91.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:pol_target_c
	right_portrait = scope:pol_support_1
	right_portrait = scope:pol_support_2
	picture = assassination
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		any_character = {
			has_character_modifier = political_power_character
			loyalty <= 30
			is_ruler = no
			popularity >= 80
			NOT = {
				has_variable = pol_coup
			}
		}
		any_character = {
			#the support
			count >= 3
			loyalty <= 30
			is_ruler = no
			OR = {
				has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				power_base >= 10
				has_character_modifier = king_maker				#in case
				has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
				AND = {
					is_general = yes
					is_mercenary = no
					is_governor = no
					power_base >= 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			tyranny >= 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			current_ruler = {
				popularity < 50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			current_ruler = {
				popularity < 25
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = political_power_character
				loyalty <= 87
				is_ruler = no
				popularity >= 20
				NOT = {
					has_variable = pol_coup
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = pol_target_c
			set_variable = {
				name = pol_coup
				days = 3650				#10y
			}
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				loyalty <= 30
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = {
					this = scope:pol_target_c
				}
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
					power_base >= 10
					has_character_modifier = king_maker					#in case
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					AND = {
						is_general = yes
						is_mercenary = no
						is_governor = no
						power_base >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = pol_support_1
			set_variable = {
				name = pol_coup
				days = 3650				#10y
			}
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				loyalty <= 30
				is_ruler = no
				NOR = {
					this = scope:pol_target_c
					this = scope:pol_support_1
				}
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
					power_base >= 10
					has_character_modifier = king_maker					#in case
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					AND = {
						is_general = yes
						is_mercenary = no
						is_governor = no
						power_base >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = pol_support_2
			set_variable = {
				name = pol_coup
				days = 3650				#10y
			}
		}
		add_stability = -8
	}
	option = {
		#accept
		name = c3rd_other_events.91.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.a.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
			add_legitimacy = -50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_republic = yes
			}
			add_political_influence = -100
		}
		scope:pol_target_c = {
			add_corruption = 25
			add_gold = {
				value = 0
				add = root.has_monthly_income
				multiply = 10
			}
		}
		every_character = {
			#the support
			limit = {
				OR = {
					loyalty <= 40
					is_friend = scope:pol_target_c
				}
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
					power_base >= 10
					has_character_modifier = king_maker					#in case
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					AND = {
						is_general = yes
						is_mercenary = no
						is_governor = no
						power_base >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = political_turmoils
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = political_turmoils
				duration = 2200
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#replace
		name = c3rd_other_events.91.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.b.tt1
		trigger = {
			current_ruler = {
				popularity <= scope:pol_target_c.popularity
			}
		}
		current_ruler = {
			death = {
				death_reason = death_execution
			}
		}
		set_as_ruler = scope:pol_target_c
		every_character = {
			#the support
			limit = {
				OR = {
					loyalty <= 40
					is_friend = scope:pol_target_c
				}
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = political_power_character
					power_base >= 10
					has_character_modifier = king_maker					#in case
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					AND = {
						is_general = yes
						is_mercenary = no
						is_governor = no
						power_base >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			add_loyalty = requests_fulfilled
		}
		add_legitimacy = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = political_turmoils
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = political_turmoils
				duration = 1400
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#fight
		name = c3rd_other_events.91.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.c.tt1
		random_list = {
			#ruler might get killed ini action
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					current_ruler = {
						martial >= 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					current_ruler = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = steadfast
							has_trait = tough
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					current_ruler = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = brain_damaged
							has_trait = blind
							has_trait = depressed
							has_trait = gout
							has_trait = limp
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					current_ruler = {
						has_trait = cautious
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					current_ruler = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = crafty
							has_trait = deceitful
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					current_ruler = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = guileless
							has_trait = incapable
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.c.tt2
				hidden_effect = {
					scope:pol_target_c = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_head_of_family = yes
							}
							add_popularity = -50
						}
						else = {
							root = {
								imprison = {
									target = scope:pol_target_c
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_legitimacy = 5
			}
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.c.tt3
				hidden_effect = {
					current_ruler = {
						death = {
							death_reason = death_assassinated
							killer = scope:pol_target_c
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_tyranny = 5
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.91.c.tt4
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = {
				#the powerful are mixed
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_friend = scope:pol_target_c
						has_character_modifier = political_power_character
						power_base >= 10
						has_character_modifier = king_maker						#in case
						has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
						AND = {
							is_general = yes
							is_mercenary = no
							is_governor = no
							power_base >= 5
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						loyalty <= 50
					}
					add_loyalty = coup_unloyal
				}
				else = {
					add_loyalty = coup_loyal
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.92 = {
	#governor complain about excessive control of another character
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.92.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.92.desc"
	left_portrait = scope:gov_owner_target_complain
	right_portrait = scope:gov_target_complain
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced		#only solidus, because i need differences with just the minor law
		NOT = {
			has_variable = recent_holding_affair_overall
		}
		any_character = {
			is_governor = yes
			is_ruler = no
			save_temporary_scope_as = gov_check_gov_owner
			NOT = {
				has_variable = recent_holding_affair
			}
			employer = {
				any_governorships = {
					governor = scope:gov_check_gov_owner
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					NOT = {
						var:governorship_owner = scope:gov_check_gov_owner
					}
					var:governorship_owner = {
						NOR = {
							is_friend = scope:gov_check_gov_owner
							family = scope:gov_check_gov_owner.family
							is_ruler = yes							#different event for ruler
						}
					}
					has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
					var:governorship_owner_ratio >= 40					#have a good grip
					region_control_value >= 10					#governor started his own puppetting
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_character = {
				is_governor = yes
				is_ruler = no
				save_temporary_scope_as = gov_check_gov_owner2
				NOT = {
					has_variable = recent_holding_affair
				}
				employer = {
					any_governorships = {
						governor = scope:gov_check_gov_owner2
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						NOT = {
							var:governorship_owner = scope:gov_check_gov_owner2
						}
						var:governorship_owner = {
							NOR = {
								is_friend = scope:gov_check_gov_owner2
								family = scope:gov_check_gov_owner2.family
								is_ruler = yes								#different event for ruler
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_character = {
				count >= 5
				is_governor = yes
				is_ruler = no
				save_temporary_scope_as = gov_check_gov_owner3
				NOT = {
					has_variable = recent_holding_affair
				}
				employer = {
					any_governorships = {
						governor = scope:gov_check_gov_owner3
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						NOT = {
							var:governorship_owner = scope:gov_check_gov_owner3
						}
						var:governorship_owner = {
							NOR = {
								is_friend = scope:gov_check_gov_owner3
								family = scope:gov_check_gov_owner3.family
								is_ruler = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_governor = yes
				is_ruler = no
				save_temporary_scope_as = gov_check_gov_owner4
				NOT = {
					has_variable = recent_holding_affair
				}
				employer = {
					any_governorships = {
						governor = scope:gov_check_gov_owner4
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						NOT = {
							var:governorship_owner = scope:gov_check_gov_owner4
							has_variable = recent_holding_affair
						}
						var:governorship_owner = {
							NOR = {
								is_friend = scope:gov_check_gov_owner4
								family = scope:gov_check_gov_owner4.family
								is_ruler = yes								#different event for ruler
							}
						}
						has_variable = governorship_owner_ratio
						var:governorship_owner_ratio >= 40						#have a good grip
						region_control_value >= 10						#governor started his own puppetting
					}
				}
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 4
					save_temporary_scope_as = govprevprev
					employer = {
						any_governorships = {
							governor = scope:govprevprev
							has_variable = governorship_owner
							NOT = {
								var:governorship_owner = scope:govprevprev
							}
							var:governorship_owner = {
								is_rival = prev.governor
								is_ruler = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = gov_target_complain
			set_variable = {
				name = recent_holding_affair
				days = 3650
			}
		}
		random_governorships = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				governor = scope:gov_target_complain
			}
			save_scope_as = govship_target_complain
			var:governorship_owner = {
				save_scope_as = gov_owner_target_complain
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = recent_holding_affair_overall
			days = 365
		}
	}
	option = {
		#yeah, let him do - owner lose popularity gain corruption, gov gain holdings
		name = c3rd_other_events.92.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.92.a.tt1
		scope:gov_owner_target_complain = {
			add_popularity = -20
			add_corruption = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_rival = scope:gov_target_complain
					}
				}
				add_rival = scope:gov_target_complain
			}
		}
		scope:gov_target_complain = {
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		add_political_influence = 10
		while = {
			count = 6
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.92.a.tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						governorship = scope:govship_target_complain
						exists = holding_owner
						holding_owner = scope:gov_owner_target_complain
					}
					holding_owner = {
						remove_holding = prev
					}
					save_scope_as = dat_holding
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
					}
					2 = {
						scope:gov_target_complain = {
							add_holding = scope:dat_holding
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:gov_owner_target_complain = {
					is_head_of_family = no
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					count < 6
					exists = holding_owner
					governorship = scope:govship_target_complain
					holding_owner = scope:gov_owner_target_complain
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					exists = holding_owner
					governorship = scope:govship_target_complain
					holding_owner = {
						is_head_of_family = yes
						family = scope:gov_owner_target_complain.family
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.92.a.tt3
		}
	}
	option = {
		#we see nothing
		name = c3rd_other_events.92.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.92.b.tt1
		add_political_influence = 30
		current_ruler = {
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		scope:gov_owner_target_complain = {
			add_loyalty = holding_protected
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no corruption in our lands ! use it to restrain both their power
		name = c3rd_other_events.92.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.92.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
		}
		scope:gov_target_complain = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:gov_owner_target_complain = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
			}
			add_tyranny = 2
		}
		while = {
			count = 6
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					governorship = scope:govship_target_complain
					exists = holding_owner
					holding_owner = scope:gov_owner_target_complain
				}
				holding_owner = {
					remove_holding = prev
				}
			}
		}
		while = {
			count = 3
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					governorship = scope:govship_target_complain
					exists = holding_owner
					holding_owner = scope:gov_target_complain
				}
				holding_owner = {
					remove_holding = prev
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:govship_target_complain = {
				calculate_the_gov_ownership = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
		}

			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.100 = {
	#apply polinf modifier
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		current_ruler = {
			has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
			has_variable = country_ownership
			OR = {
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 30
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner20
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 40
					var:country_ownership >= 30
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner30
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 50
					var:country_ownership >= 40
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner40
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 60
					var:country_ownership >= 50
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner50
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 70
					var:country_ownership >= 60
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner60
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership < 80
					var:country_ownership >= 70
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner70
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					var:country_ownership >= 80
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner80
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 30
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner20
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_polinf_modifiers = yes
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = polinf_ruler_owner20
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 40
					var:country_ownership >= 30
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_polinf_modifiers = yes
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = polinf_ruler_owner30
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 50
					var:country_ownership >= 40
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner40
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_polinf_modifiers = yes
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = polinf_ruler_owner40
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 60
					var:country_ownership >= 50
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner50
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_polinf_modifiers = yes
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = polinf_ruler_owner50
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 70
					var:country_ownership >= 60
					root = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = polinf_ruler_owner60
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_polinf_modifiers = yes
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = polinf_ruler_owner60
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				current_ruler = {
					has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
					has_variable = country_ownership
					var:country_ownership < 80
					var:country_ownership >= 70
					root = {

c3rd_other_events.101 = {
	#good ruler can make the 2nd admin law available
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.101.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.101.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 750.1.1
		NOR = {
			has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
			has_variable = constantine_reform_available
			has_variable = tried_reform_constantine
			has_law = constantine_reform_law
			invention = administrative_military_reform_c3rd
		}
		has_variable = recent_military_anarchy
		current_ruler = {
			finesse >= 10
			charisma >= 5
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			ruler = {
				finesse >= 12
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			ruler = {
				finesse >= 15
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			ruler = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = wise
					has_trait = scholar
					has_trait = intelligent
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = tried_reform_constantine
			days = 7300
		}
	}
	option = {
		#yes ! let's do this
		name = c3rd_other_events.101.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.101.a.tt1
		add_political_influence = -20
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 20
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = constantine_reform_available
		}
	}
	option = {
		#we'll lose the ownership
		name = c3rd_other_events.101.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.101.b.tt1
		add_political_influence = 5
		add_legitimacy = 5
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.103 = {
	#duchy subject no longer a duchy
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.103.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.103.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = throneroom
	trigger = {
		any_subject = {
			is_subject_type = duchy_subject
			NOT = {
				government = duchy
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_subject = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_type = duchy_subject
				NOT = {
					government = duchy
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = ex_duchy
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			release_subject = scope:ex_duchy
		}
	}
	option = {
		#client
		name = c3rd_other_events.103.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.103.a.tt1
		make_subject = {
			target = scope:ex_duchy
			type = client_state
		}
		scope:ex_duchy = {
			set_variable = {
				name = recent_client
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#tributary
		name = c3rd_other_events.103.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.103.b.tt1
		make_subject = {
			target = scope:ex_duchy
			type = tributary
		}
		scope:ex_duchy = {
			set_variable = {
				name = subject_wants_more_cooldown
				days = 3650
			}
		}
		add_stability = 2
		add_tyranny = -3
	}
	option = {
		#ally
		name = c3rd_other_events.103.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.103.c.tt1
		scope:ex_duchy = {
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = empire_gave_independance
				target = root
			}
		}
		add_opinion = {
			modifier = empire_gave_independance
			target = scope:ex_duchy
		}
		add_stability = 5
		add_aggressive_expansion = -10
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.105 = {
	#heritage of big landowner
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.105.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.105.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = throneroom
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 750.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		any_character = {
			employer = root
			has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
			has_variable = potential_sucession_ownership_crisis
			save_temporary_scope_as = main_heir_landowner1
			family = {
				any_family_member = {
					count >= 3
					is_adult = yes
					employer = root
					NOT = {
						this = scope:main_heir_landowner1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_stability = -10
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				employer = root
				has_character_modifier = major_influence_aristocrat
				has_variable = potential_sucession_ownership_crisis
				save_temporary_scope_as = main_heir_landowner2
				family = {
					any_family_member = {
						count >= 3
						is_adult = yes
						employer = root
						NOT = {
							this = scope:main_heir_landowner2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = main_heir_landowner
			remove_variable = potential_sucession_ownership_crisis
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				employer = root
				NOT = {
					this = scope:main_heir_landowner
				}
				family = scope:main_heir_landowner.family
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_heir_landowner
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				employer = root
				NOR = {
					this = scope:main_heir_landowner
					this = scope:second_heir_landowner
				}
				family = scope:main_heir_landowner.family
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = third_heir_landowner
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				employer = root
				NOR = {
					this = scope:main_heir_landowner
					this = scope:second_heir_landowner
					this = scope:third_heir_landowner
				}
				family = scope:main_heir_landowner.family
			}
			weight = {
				modifier = {
					add = power_base
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = fourth_heir_landowner
		}
	}
	option = {
		#main heir
		name = c3rd_other_events.105.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.105.a.tt1
		add_tyranny = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:main_heir_landowner = {
					is_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = -10
		}
		scope:main_heir_landowner = {
			add_loyalty = coup_loyal
		}
		scope:second_heir_landowner = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
		scope:third_heir_landowner = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
		scope:fourth_heir_landowner = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
	}
	option = {
		#share
		name = c3rd_other_events.105.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.105.b.tt1
		hidden_effect = {
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = scope:main_heir_landowner
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:second_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:second_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:third_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:third_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:fourth_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:fourth_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_subject = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_type = autonomous_domain
					has_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					var:owner_from_another_empire = scope:main_heir_landowner
				}
				1 = {
				}
				1 = {
					remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					set_variable = {
						name = owner_from_another_empire
						value = scope:second_heir_landowner
					}
				}
				1 = {
					remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					set_variable = {
						name = owner_from_another_empire
						value = scope:third_heir_landowner
					}
				}
				1 = {
					remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					set_variable = {
						name = owner_from_another_empire
						value = scope:fourth_heir_landowner
					}
				}
			}
		}
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:main_heir_landowner = {
					is_ruler = no
				}
			}
			add_stability = -5
		}
		add_tyranny = -5
	}
	option = {
		#get the country's share
		name = c3rd_other_events.105.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.105.c.tt1
		hidden_effect = {
			every_governorships = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = scope:main_heir_landowner
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:second_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:second_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:third_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:third_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						set_variable = {
							name = governorship_owner
							value = scope:fourth_heir_landowner
						}
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
								scope:fourth_heir_landowner = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						remove_variable = governorship_owner
						every_governorship_state = {
							every_state_province = {
								limit = {
									exists = holding_owner
									holding_owner = {
										this = scope:main_heir_landowner
									}
								}
								scope:main_heir_landowner = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_subject = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_type = autonomous_domain
					has_variable = owner_from_another_empire

				1 = {

					remove_variable = owner_from_another_empire
					set_variable = {
						name = owner_from_another_empire
						value = scope:second_heir_landowner
					}

					}

c3rd_other_events.106 = {
	#Consolidate, coveted owner heads want in their family
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.106.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.106.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	left_portrait = scope:minor_owner
	right_portrait = scope:first_head_pretender
	right_portrait = scope:second_head_pretender
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 750.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		any_character = {
			employer = root
			is_minor_character = yes
			save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_minor_owner
			NOR = {
				any_rival = {
					has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
				}
				has_variable = got_pretended_owner
			}
			root = {
				any_governorships = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					var:governorship_owner = scope:tmp_minor_owner
				}
			}
		}
		any_character = {
			count >= 2
			is_head_of_family = yes
			has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_character = {
				count >= 3
				employer = root
				is_minor_character = yes
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_minor_owner
				NOR = {
					any_rival = {
						has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					}
					has_variable = got_pretended_owner
				}
				root = {
					any_governorships = {
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = scope:tmp_minor_owner
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_character = {
				count >= 5
				employer = root
				is_minor_character = yes
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_minor_owner
				NOR = {
					any_rival = {
						has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					}
					has_variable = got_pretended_owner
				}
				root = {
					any_governorships = {
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = scope:tmp_minor_owner
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_cities >= 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_owned_province = {
				count <= country_size_ratio
				NOT = {
					exists = holding_owner
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				employer = root
				is_minor_character = yes
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_minor_owner
				NOR = {
					any_rival = {
						has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
					}
					has_variable = got_pretended_owner
				}
				root = {
					any_governorships = {
						has_variable = governorship_owner
						var:governorship_owner = scope:tmp_minor_owner
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = minor_owner
			set_variable = {
				name = got_pretended_owner
				days = 1850
			}
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
			}
			save_scope_as = first_head_pretender
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				has_variable = head_intent_consolidate
				NOT = {
					this = scope:first_head_pretender
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_head_pretender
		}
	}
	option = {
		#favour 1
		name = c3rd_other_events.106.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.106.a.tt1
		scope:minor_owner = {
			set_family = scope:first_head_pretender.family
		}
		scope:first_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = supported_action
		}
		scope:second_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
	option = {
		#favour 2
		name = c3rd_other_events.106.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.106.b.tt1
		scope:minor_owner = {
			set_family = scope:second_head_pretender.family
		}
		scope:first_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:second_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = supported_action
		}
	}
	option = {
		#NONE
		name = c3rd_other_events.106.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.106.c.tt1
		add_legitimacy = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			add_tyranny = 2
		}
		scope:minor_owner = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:first_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:second_head_pretender = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
	after = {
		scope:first_head_pretender = {
			remove_variable = head_intent_consolidate
		}
		scope:second_head_pretender = {
			remove_variable = head_intent_consolidate
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.107 = {
	#disloyal head
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.107.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.107.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	right_portrait = scope:first_head_disloyal
	right_portrait = scope:second_head_disloyal
	picture = roman_trial
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 750.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		NOT = {
			has_variable = got_disloyal_heads
		}
		any_character = {
			count >= 2
			is_head_of_family = yes
			has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
		}
		any_governorships = {
			NOR = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				has_variable = got_disloyal_head
			}
			save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_gowship_check
			owner = {
				any_owned_province = {
					count >= 10
					governorship = scope:tmp_gowship_check
					exists = holding_owner
					holding_owner = {
						this = root.current_ruler
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_governorships = {
				count >= 3
				NOR = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					has_variable = got_disloyal_head
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_gowship_check
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						count >= 10
						governorship = scope:tmp_gowship_check
						exists = holding_owner
						holding_owner = {
							this = root.current_ruler
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_governorships = {
				count >= 5
				NOR = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					has_variable = got_disloyal_head
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_gowship_check
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						count >= 10
						governorship = scope:tmp_gowship_check
						exists = holding_owner
						holding_owner = {
							this = root.current_ruler
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			num_of_cities >= 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			towards_civil_war = yes
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_governorships = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_variable = governorship_owner
					has_variable = got_disloyal_head
				}
				save_temporary_scope_as = tmp_gowship_check
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						count >= 10
						governorship = scope:tmp_gowship_check
						exists = holding_owner
						holding_owner = {
							this = root.current_ruler
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = target_governorship
			set_variable = {
				name = got_disloyal_head
				days = 1850
			}
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
			}
			save_scope_as = first_head_disloyal
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
				NOT = {
					this = scope:first_head_disloyal
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = second_head_disloyal
		}
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				has_variable = head_intent_loyal
			}
			save_scope_as = loyal_head
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = got_disloyal_heads
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#okay
		name = c3rd_other_events.107.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.107.a.tt1
		add_legitimacy = -5
		scope:target_governorship = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					name = recently_gavaway
					days = 365
				}
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {
						limit = {
							exists = holding_owner
							holding_owner = {
								this = root.current_ruler
							}
						}
						root.current_ruler = {
							remove_holding = prev
						}
						random_list = {
							2 = {
							}
							3 = {
								scope:first_head_disloyal = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
							3 = {
								scope:second_head_disloyal = {
									add_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#no !
		name = c3rd_other_events.107.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.107.b.tt1
		add_tyranny = 5
		add_stability = -5
		scope:first_head_disloyal = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
		scope:second_head_disloyal = {
			add_loyalty = medium_requests_denied
		}
	}
	option = {
		#help me
		name = c3rd_other_events.107.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.107.c.tt1
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:loyal_head
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_legitimacy = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			add_tyranny = 2
		}
		add_political_influence = -5
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_cities <= 1000
			}
			scope:first_head_disloyal = {
				remove_variable = head_intent_disloyal
			}
			scope:second_head_disloyal = {
				remove_variable = head_intent_disloyal
			}
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.110 = {
	#Intervention
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.110.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.110.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler

	right_portrait = scope:second_inter_char
	right_portrait = scope:third_inter_char
	picture = roman_trial
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		num_of_cities >= 400		#the 400-500 buffer
		NOT = {
			has_variable = recent_intervention
		}
		any_character = {
			#minimum = 1 head of family is disloyal
			is_head_of_family = yes
			loyalty < 33
		}
		OR = {
			disloyal_country_part >= 60
			any_character = {
				#we need 3 characters at the very least that are disloyal and either : heavy general in milanarch, king maker, own 25% of the country, powerbase >10 no general, powerbase >10 general with milanarch possible and unworthy_leader > 3
				count >= 3
				OR = {
					loyalty < 33
					AND = {
						has_variable = head_intent_disloyal
						loyalty <= 45
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_head_of_family = yes
					AND = {
						is_general = yes
						is_governor = no
						power_base > 5
						employer = {
							has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
						}

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

						has_variable = unworthy_leader
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = unworthy_leader
						add = 4
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = {
						name = unworthy_leader
						value = 4
					}
				}
				current_ruler = {
					add_popularity = -25
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = decentralized_administration_law
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
				add_legitimacy = -15
			}
			else = {
				add_political_influence = -30
			}
		}
		if = {
			#in milanarch, every general is not happy
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = military_anarchy
			}
			current_ruler = {
				add_popularity = -25
			}
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						this = scope:first_inter_char
						this = scope:second_inter_char
						this = scope:third_inter_char
					}
					is_general = yes
				}
				add_loyalty = disappointed
			}
		}
		scope:first_inter_char = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:second_inter_char = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
		scope:third_inter_char = {
			add_loyalty = disappointed
		}
	}
	after = {
		every_governorships = {
			limit = {
				is_in_list = family_domain_govs
			}
			remove_from_list = family_domain_govs
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.120 = {
	#ruler extremely corrupted
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.120.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.120.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = greek_court
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 600.1.1
		current_ruler = {
			corruption >= 80
		}
		NOR = {
			has_variable = recent_ruler_corrupted
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			current_ruler = {
				corruption >= 90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			current_ruler = {
				corruption >= 95
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			current_ruler = {
				corruption >= 99
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = recent_ruler_corrupted
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#go uncorrupted
		name = c3rd_other_events.120.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.120.a.tt1
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -10
			add_corruption = -5
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = fight_global_corruption
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#go corrupted
		name = c3rd_other_events.120.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.120.b.tt1
		add_stability = 5
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = 10
			add_corruption = 5
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = {
				is_head_of_family = yes
				is_ruler = no
			}
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = encourage_global_corruption
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
	option = {
		#don't move
		name = c3rd_other_events.120.c
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.120.c.tt1
		add_stability = -6
		add_tyranny = 5
		add_political_influence = -25
		add_legitimacy = -20
		current_ruler = {
			add_popularity = -25
			add_corruption = 10
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = ruler_goes_corruption_unchecked
			days = 3650
		}
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.130 = {
	#EPIDEMY owners take control
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.130.t"
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			#owner is ruler
			trigger = {
				scope:owner_epidemy_action = {
					is_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.130.desc.1"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#owner is smart : less mortality, but less taxes and trade
			trigger = {
				scope:owner_epidemy_action = {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = cruel
						has_trait = selfish
						has_trait = corrupt
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.130.desc.2"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			#owner is cruel : provincila loyalty and mortality
			trigger = {
				scope:owner_epidemy_action = {
					NOT = {
						is_ruler = yes
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = cruel
						has_trait = selfish
						has_trait = corrupt
					}
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.130.desc.3"
		}
	}
	left_portrait = scope:owner_epidemy_action
	picture = senator_conversing
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 600.1.1
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = "antonine_plague_epidemic_outbreak_city"
				has_province_modifier = "antonine_plague_epidemic_quarantine"
				has_province_modifier = "plague_outbreak_province"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_outbreak_city"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_quarantine"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_outbreak_town"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_quarantown"
			}
			state = {
				NOR = {
					has_state_modifier = c3rd_epidemy_cruel
					has_state_modifier = c3rd_epidemy_normal
					has_state_modifier = c3rd_epidemy_ruler
				}
			}
			governorship = {
				has_variable = governorship_owner
				var:governorship_owner = {
					employer = root
				}
				NOR = {
					has_variable = recent_epidemy_owner_choice
					var:governorship_owner = {
						has_variable = recent_epidemy_owner_choice_char
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	weight_multiplier = {
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

			limit = {

			}

			add_political_influence = -25
		}
	}

				}
				every_governorship_state = {
					every_state_province = {

							2 = {
							}
							3 = {
								root.current_ruler = {
									remove_holding = prev
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

c3rd_other_events.131 = {
	#EPIDEMY modifier event when solidus (you enacted solidus too soon event type)
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.131.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.131.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 700.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		any_owned_province = {
			count >= 10
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = "antonine_plague_epidemic_outbreak_city"
				has_province_modifier = "antonine_plague_epidemic_quarantine"
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = already_epidemy_modifier_solidus_1
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = epidemy_modifier_solidus_1
			duration = 14600			#40 years
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = already_epidemy_modifier_solidus_1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.131.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.131.a.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.132 = {
	#EPIDEMY modifier 2 event when solidus (you enacted solidus too soon event type)
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.132.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.132.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		any_owned_province = {
			count >= 10
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_outbreak_city"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_quarantine"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_outbreak_town"
				has_province_modifier = "cyprian_plague_epidemic_quarantown"
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = already_epidemy_modifier_solidus_2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = epidemy_modifier_solidus_2
			duration = 14600			#40 years
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = already_epidemy_modifier_solidus_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.132.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.132.a.tt1
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.140 = {
	#losing permanent modifiers
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.140.t"
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.140.desc.1"
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
				}
			}
			desc = "c3rd_other_events.140.desc.2"
		}
	}
	picture = hellenic_temple
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		NOT = {
			has_variable = recent_lost_glory
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = heirs_of_alexander
			has_country_modifier = egypt_mediterranean_lord
			has_country_modifier = argead_empire_modifier
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				any_country = {
					has_variable = mother_empire
					var:mother_empire = root
					NOT = {
						has_variable = recent_empire_split
					}
				}
				stability <= 35
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_modifier = internal_collapse
				has_country_modifier = c3rd_border_pressure
			}
			AND = {
				current_date >= 1000.1.1
				has_country_modifier = c3rd_border_pressure
				stability <= 25
			}
			AND = {
				current_date >= 1100.1.1
				has_country_modifier = c3rd_border_pressure
				stability <= 30
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = recent_lost_glory
			days = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = heirs_of_alexander
			}
			remove_country_modifier = heirs_of_alexander
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = argead_empire_modifier
			}
			remove_country_modifier = argead_empire_modifier
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = egypt_mediterranean_lord
			}
			remove_country_modifier = egypt_mediterranean_lord
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = c3rd_other_events.140.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.140.a.tt1
		add_stability = 5
	}
}

c3rd_other_events.141 = {
	#change bureaucracy modifiers
	type = country_event
	title = "c3rd_other_events.141.t"
	desc = "c3rd_other_events.141.desc"
	left_portrait = current_ruler
	picture = successors
	trigger = {
		has_land = yes
		is_tribal = no
		has_civil_war = no
		current_date >= 800.1.1
		has_country_modifier = solidus_introduced
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = appointed_bureaucracy
			has_country_modifier = meritocratic_bureaucracy
			has_country_modifier = noble_bureaucracy
		}
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		#keep the modifier
		name = c3rd_other_events.141.a
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.141.a.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = appointed_bureaucracy
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = appointed_bureaucracy
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = late_appointed_bureaucracy
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = meritocratic_bureaucracy
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = meritocratic_bureaucracy
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = late_meritocratic_bureaucracy
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = noble_bureaucracy
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_country_modifier = noble_bureaucracy
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = late_noble_bureaucracy
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#new modifier
		name = c3rd_other_events.141.b
		custom_tooltip = c3rd_other_events.141.b.tt1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = appointed_bureaucracy
			}
			remove_country_modifier = appointed_bureaucracy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = meritocratic_bureaucracy
			}
			remove_country_modifier = meritocratic_bureaucracy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = noble_bureaucracy
			}
			remove_country_modifier = noble_bureaucracy
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = late_bureaucracy_c3rd
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
